### [120] [Novel Aspects of IEEE SA P3109 Arithmetic Formats for Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04028)
*Andrew Fitzgibbon,Christoph M. Wintersteiger,Jeffrey Sarnoff*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IEEE P3109 草案定义了一套针对机器学习优化的参数化二进制浮点格式与运算规范，通过简化异常处理、支持块级缩放及形式化验证，旨在提升数值计算的效率与一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的浮点标准（如 IEEE 754）在处理低位宽、机器学习特定需求（如块级缩放、高效吞吐）方面不够灵活，IEEE P3109 旨在定义一套标准化的浮点格式及运算，以支持机器学习推理和训练中的高效计算。

Method: 该标准采用参数化设计（参数包括位宽、精度、有符号性等），通过将浮点值解码为闭扩展实数集来定义运算；引入了包括随机舍入在内的多种舍入与饱和模式；定义了无异常运算架构，并通过返回值（如 NaN）处理异常；提出了“kappa-近似”尺度不变度量，并利用形式化规格进行机械验证。

Result: IEEE P3109 建立了一套灵活的、可参数化的浮点数体系，确保了算术操作的一致性与可验证性，同时通过无异常运算设计提升了硬件处理效率，为机器学习算力优化提供了标准化的技术参考。

Conclusion: IEEE P3109 草案通过定义参数化的二进制浮点格式与运算规范，为机器学习领域提供了统一、高效且标准化的计算基础，有助于在不同硬件实现间保持数值一致性。

Abstract: The IEEE P3109 draft standard defines a parameterized family of binary floating-point formats and associated operations, with a focus on facilitating machine learning. These formats allow efficient and consistent representation of values in a small number of bits. The defined formats are parameterized over width and precision in bits, signedness, and the presence of infinities. Operations are defined by decoding floating-point values to the set of closed extended reals: the reals augmented with positive and negative infinity and NaN (Not a Number). Explicit treatment of NaN and infinite operands ensures that only real arithmetic is invoked in operation definitions. Extensive rounding and saturation modes are defined; stochastic rounding is included. Operations are exception-free, accelerating throughput, with exceptional situations communicated through return values, e.g., NaN. Operations on blocks of values sharing a common scale factor are defined in terms of the underlying operations in a uniform manner. System vendors may describe approximate implementations via a novel scale-invariant measure, akin to units in the last place, called kappa-approximation. Standard function definitions and various other properties are mechanically verified and generated using formal specifications.

</details>


### [121] [Position: Deployed Reinforcement Learning should be Continual](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04029)
*Parnian Behdin,Kevin Roice,Golnaz Mesbahi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文批判了强化学习中常见的“先训练后固定”范式，指出现实世界的动态性要求代理具备持续学习（Never-ending learning）的能力，并呼吁学术界向持续强化学习方向转型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前强化学习在现实世界中多采用“先训练后固定”的范式，即代理在部署后不再学习。作者认为这种模式无法处理现实世界中环境不断变化带来的非平稳性问题，因此需要建立能够持续适应的强化学习系统。

Method: 本文是一篇观点论文（Position Paper），通过分析强化学习在现实世界部署中面临的挑战，识别了部署后导致非平稳性的四个来源，并结合成功案例研究，阐述了持续强化学习（Continual RL）的理论必要性及其实施策略。

Result: 明确了部署后影响代理性能的四类非平稳性因素，论证了代理持续学习对于保持长期最优性能的核心价值，并为社区摆脱静态部署模式提供了指导思路。

Conclusion: 论文主张放弃“先训练后固定”的传统模式，转向持续强化学习。强调了在部署环境中，为了应对非平稳性并保持性能最优，代理程序必须具备持续学习的能力，并提出了实现这一范式转变的必要性和潜在路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has received increasing attention and adoption in real-world use cases. Most of these systems follow a train-then-fix paradigm, where trained agents do not learn while interacting with the world until performance degrades and retraining becomes necessary. In this position paper, we argue that deploying an agent that is incapable of optimality, but receives an evaluative reward signal, is inherently a continual RL problem. We identify four sources of non-stationarity after deployment that necessitate never-ending learning, and highlight why the best deployed agents never stop adapting. We analyze successful examples of continual RL in the real world, and present the community with the advantages and measures to move away from the current train-then-fix paradigm.

</details>


### [122] [Do Transformers Need Three Projections? Systematic Study of QKV Variants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04032)
*Ali Kayyam,Anusha Madan Gopal,M Anthony Lewis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统性地验证了在 Transformer 注意力机制中共享 QKV 投影矩阵的可行性。研究发现通过 Q-K=V 共享，可以在几乎不影响模型性能的同时，大幅缩减 KV 缓存，并能与现有的分组查询注意力（GQA/MQA）技术叠加，显著提升大模型的端侧部署能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 Transformer 在人工智能领域占据主导地位，但 QKV 注意力机制中三个投影矩阵各自的必要性及其相互作用尚不明确。研究旨在探究减少投影矩阵的数量是否能降低推理时的显存消耗（特别是 KV 缓存），并评估其对模型性能的影响，以解决端侧部署的存储瓶颈。

Method: 研究人员系统地评估了三种 QKV 投影共享约束：1) Q-K=V（共享键值），2) Q=K-V（共享查询键），以及 3) Q=K=V（单一投影）。针对对称注意力图问题，采用了 2D 位置编码以引入非对称性，并在合成任务、视觉任务（MNIST、CIFAR 等）及大规模语言模型（300M/1.2B 参数）上进行了广泛的实证研究。

Result: 实验发现，简化投影架构后的 Transformer 模型表现与标准 QKV 结构相当甚至更好。在语言模型中，Q-K=V 共享策略在仅损失 3.1% 困惑度（perplexity）的情况下，将 KV 缓存减少了 50%；若与 GQA-4 或 MQA 结合，KV 缓存降幅分别达到 87.5% 和 96.9%，为高效端侧推理提供了极具价值的方案。

Conclusion: 研究表明，Transformer 中的投影共享是一种未被充分利用的权重绑定策略。通过 Q=K 共享，可以在几乎不损失性能的前提下显著减少 KV 缓存需求，特别是在与 GQA/MQA 结合时，能够极大提升端侧设备的推理效率。此外，研究揭示了注意力机制在低秩状态下运行，且键（Key）和值（Value）占据相似的表示空间。

Abstract: Transformers have become the standard solution for various AI tasks, with the query, key, and value (QKV) attention formulation playing a central role. However, the individual contribution of these three projections and the impact of omitting some remain poorly understood. We systematically evaluate three projection sharing constraints: a) Q-K=V (shared key-value), b) Q=K-V (shared query-key), and c) Q=K=V (single projection). The last two variants produce symmetric attention maps; to address this, we also explore asymmetric attention via 2D positional encodings. Through experiments spanning synthetic tasks, vision (MNIST, CIFAR, TinyImageNet, anomaly), and language modeling (300M and 1.2B parameter models on 10B tokens), we discovered that our transformers perform on par or occasionally better than the QKV transformer. In language modeling, Q-K=V projection sharing achieves 50% KV cache reduction with only 3.1% perplexity degradation. Crucially, projection sharing is complementary to head sharing (GQA/MQA): combining Q-K=V with GQA-4 yields 87.5% cache reduction, while Q-K=V + MQA achieves 96.9%, enabling practical on-device inference. We show that Q-K=V preserves quality because keys and values can occupy similar representational spaces and attention operates in a low-rank regime, whereas Q=K-V breaks attention directionality. Our results systematically characterize projection sharing as an underexplored instance of weight tying in attention, with direct, quantifiable inference memory benefits, particularly valuable for edge deployment. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/anushamadan02/Do-Transformers-Need-3-Projections

</details>


### [123] [Inverse Critical Experiment Design via Gradient Optimization and a Multigroup Attention-Based Neural Network Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04033)
*Will Savage,Logan Burnett,Dean Price*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度神经网络代理模型和梯度优化的逆向设计方法，用于自动生成与目标核反应堆设计具有高物理相似度的关键实验布局，从而加速先进核技术的实验验证过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先进核反应堆设计与燃料概念的验证依赖于与目标技术具有高物理相似性的关键实验。然而，手动设计这些实验以达到所需的相似度标准（$c_k \geq 0.9$）既耗时又困难。因此，需要一种自动化的逆向设计方法来生成能最大化相似度指标的实验几何配置。

Method: 1. 构建基于深度神经网络的代理模型，用于预测核数据不确定性引起的有效增殖因子（$k_{eff}$）偏置相关系数（$c_k$）；
2. 采用结合U-Net编码器-解码器与多组注意力池化（Multigroup Attention Pooling）层的新型架构，以捕获空间敏感性；
3. 利用代理模型的可微性，通过非参数梯度优化方法，直接在组合设计空间内调整几何网格的材料分配，实现$c_k$的最大化。

Result: 该方法在针对TN-Americas TN-LC运输桶（使用HALEU燃料）的验证应用中表现出色。对于三个特定的感兴趣配置，优化后的几何布局分别取得了0.97757、0.81324和0.93276的$c_k$分数，证明了该方法在生成高相似度实验方案方面的卓越能力。

Conclusion: 本研究成功验证了深度学习辅助的逆向设计方法在核反应堆关键实验设计中的有效性。通过将深度神经网络与梯度优化结合，能够高效生成满足高相似度要求（$c_k \geq 0.9$）的实验几何布局。该方法为先进核技术（如HALEU燃料运输）的验证提供了强有力的工具，显著缩短了实验设计周期。

Abstract: The validation of advanced nuclear reactor designs and fuel concepts requires critical experiments with high neutronic similarity to the target technology. Neutronic similarity is quantified by the correlation coefficient $c_k$, which captures the shared bias in $k_\text{eff}$ induced by uncertainties in nuclear data. Generally, a $c_k\geq0.9$ is needed for an experiment to be sufficiently similar to a target technology. This work presents a methodology for the inverse design of critical experiments. Deep neural network surrogate modeling and nonparametric gradient optimization are used to generate experiment geometries that maximize $c_k$.
  A deep neural network is trained on OpenMC-calculated sensitivity vectors for grid-based critical experiment geometries. The model architecture combines a U-Net convolutional encoder-decoder with a novel multigroup attention pooling layer, introduced to capture the differing spatial dependencies of sensitivities. Multigroup attention pooling is shown to achieve better performance than traditional pooling, as well as interpretable internal behavior. The differentiability of the surrogate enables gradient-based optimization of the full combinatorial design space, allowing $c_k$ to be maximized by directly changing the material assignment of each position in the geometry grid.
  The method is applied to the validation of the TN-Americas TN-LC transportation cask with HALEU fuel, for which existing critical experiment coverage is limited. The optimization procedure is shown to produce experiment geometries achieving $c_k$ scores of 0.97757, 0.81324, and 0.93276 for three configurations of interest. This approach demonstrates the potential of deep learning and gradient optimization to accelerate the development of advanced nuclear technology.

### [124] [Self-Distilled Policy Gradient](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04036)
*Yifeng Liu,Shiyuan Zhang,Yifan Zhang,Quanquan Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SDPG 是一种结合了全词表自蒸馏、组相对奖励和正则化策略的强化学习框架，旨在解决语言模型在稀疏奖励场景下的学习效率与稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种自蒸馏策略梯度框架（SDPG），该方法包含三个核心组件：1. 组相对验证器优势（Group-relative verifier advantages）与正规化标准差；2. 精确的全词表同策略自蒸馏（Exact full-vocabulary on-policy self-distillation）；3. 参考策略 KL 正则化。

Result: 实验结果表明，SDPG 在性能和训练稳定性方面均优于现有的 RLVR（Reinforcement Learning from Verifier Rewards）和传统的自蒸馏基准方法。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation, where a language model conditions on privileged context to supervise its own generations, is a promising source of dense supervision for sparse-reward reinforcement learning. Actually, it can be instantiated as an auxiliary full-vocabulary student-to-teacher reverse Kullback-Leibler divergence loss. We therefore propose SDPG, a self-distilled policy-gradient framework that combines group-relative verifier advantages with normalized standard deviation, exact full-vocabulary on-policy self-distillation, as well as reference-policy KL regularization. Empirically, SDPG improves stability and performance over RLVR and self-distillation baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/lauyikfung/SDPG.

### [125] [Bayes-Sufficient Representations in Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04045)
*Vasileios Sevetlidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文从决策理论视角重新审视了监督学习中的表征学习，定义了“贝叶斯充分性”和“贝叶斯极小性”，证明了最优表征不仅依赖于数据分布，还直接受损失函数约束，从而为衡量表征是否包含冗余信息提供了数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的表征学习通常含糊地定义为“保留对预测相关的信息”。该研究旨在量化这种“相关性”的定义，探讨在给定的监督学习任务和损失函数下，到底需要什么样的信息才能实现贝叶斯最优决策。

Method: 该研究提出了“贝叶斯充分性（Bayes-sufficiency）”的概念，利用决策理论中的“贝叶斯商（Bayes quotient）”来定义特定损失函数下所需的最小化信息。研究将表征学习与性质诱导（property elicitation）理论相结合，并通过控制实验、神经瓶颈模型以及iNaturalist生物分类数据集进行了实证分析。

Result: 研究证明了在特定损失函数下（如0-1损失、平方损失、对数损失等），表征是否充分取决于它是否精炼了相应的贝叶斯商。实证结果显示，通过该框架可以准确区分模型保留的必要信息、冗余信息以及对贝叶斯最优决策至关重要的信息，从而实现对模型表征能力的深度评估。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了一个严谨的决策理论框架，指出监督学习中的表征学习不仅取决于数据分布，还必须结合特定的损失函数。通过区分贝叶斯充分性（Bayes-sufficiency）与贝叶斯极小性（Bayes-minimality），该框架为评估模型是否保留了不必要的冗余信息提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Representation learning is often described as preserving the information in an input that is relevant for prediction. This work asks what relevance means for a fixed supervised decision problem. A representation is defined to be Bayes-sufficient for a joint distribution and loss if some prediction head can use it to implement a Bayes-optimal action rule. This makes the target information loss-dependent. In the almost-surely unique Bayes-action case, the relevant object is a Bayes quotient, which identifies inputs that require the same Bayes-optimal action. A representation is sufficient when it refines this quotient, and Bayes-minimal when it is informationally equivalent to it. The framework connects naturally to property elicitation: zero-one loss requires the Bayes class, squared loss the conditional mean, Brier loss the conditional probability in binary prediction, and log loss or strictly proper scoring rules the predictive distribution. Controlled finite experiments, learned neural bottleneck experiments, and a real-data iNaturalist taxonomic refinement experiment illustrate the distinction between sufficiency, minimality, and retained non-required information. For a fixed supervised problem, the distribution and the loss determine the Bayes action, the Bayes action determines the quotient, and the quotient determines the minimal information required for Bayes-optimal prediction.

</details>

Method: 研究者通过严格推导，将坐标大小估计（coordinate-size estimates）传播至模型的前向传播过程、门控机制以及递归状态动态中，从而推导出了适用于门控Delta网络的特定缩放规则（Scaling rules）。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论推导和实验验证，成功将μP（最大化更新参数化）扩展到了门控Delta网络（Gated Delta Network），证明了该方法在处理复杂循环结构和门控机制时，能够有效实现跨模型规模的超参数零样本迁移，为高效训练新型亚二次复杂度模型提供了坚实的理论支持。

Abstract: Training and scaling Large Language Models demand enormous computational resources, motivating both efficient sub-quadratic architectures and principled hyperparameter tuning methods. While the Maximal Update Parametrization ($μ$P) has enabled zero-shot hyperparameter transfer for standard Transformers, its extension to linear models, particularly those with structured state transitions and complicated architectures, remains largely unexplored. By rigorously propagating coordinate-size estimates through the forward pass, gating mechanisms, and recurrent state dynamics, we derive the scaling rules for Gated Delta Network. Experiments on language-model pre-training confirm that our configurations enable stable learning-rate transfer across model widths under both AdamW and SGD, whereas standard parametrization fails to transfer, validating the correctness and practical utility of our analysis.

### [127] [LiftQuant: Continuous Bit-Width LLM via Dimensional Lifting and Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04050)
*Liulu He,XuanAng Liu,Juntao Liu,Taolue Feng,Ting Lu,Chunsheng Gan,Zhiyv Peng,Yuan Du,Huanrui Yang,Yijiang Liu,Li Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LiftQuant 是一种新型大模型量化框架，通过“提升-投影”机制打破了整数位宽的限制，实现了准连续的位宽调节，能够在任意内存预算下达到最优性能，同时保持了高效的硬件执行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量化方法受限于固定的整数位宽（如 2-bit、3-bit），导致大语言模型在适配特定硬件内存预算时存在“部署缺口”，无法达到帕累托最优状态。

Method: 引入“提升-投影”（lift-then-project）机制：通过将低维权重向量投影到高维“提升”空间中的简单 1-bit 格点，利用提升维度与原始维度的比例关系来灵活控制有效位宽，从而生成具备矢量量化（VQ）表达能力且保持线性转换计算路径的非均匀码本。

Result: LiftQuant 成功将 70B 参数的大语言模型压缩至 2.4 bits，使其能够精准适配 24GB 显存，且在相同硬件约束下，其性能显著优于当前最先进的 2-bit 量化模型。

Conclusion: LiftQuant 提出了一种创新的“提升-投影”量化框架，通过灵活调整提升空间的维度，实现了量化位宽的准连续调节。该方法不仅填补了传统整数位宽量化方法在特定内存限制下的“部署缺口”，还兼顾了高性能与硬件友好性，为大模型的轻量化部署提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Existing quantization methods are fundamentally limited by rigid, integer-based bit-widths (e.g., 2, 3-bit), resulting in a ``deployment gap" where Large Language Models cannot be optimally fitted to specific memory budgets. To bridge this gap, we introduce LiftQuant, a novel framework that enables continuous bit-width control for true Pareto-optimal deployment. The core innovation is a ``lift-then-project" mechanism which approximates low-dimensional weight vectors by projecting a simple 1-bit lattice from a higher-dimensional ``lifted" space. Crucially, the effective bit-width is determined simply by the ratio of the lifted dimension to the original dimension, which allows the bit-width to be tuned quasi-continuous as the dimension is a flexible structural parameter. This projection generates a structured yet non-uniform codebook, capturing the expressive power of Vector Quantization (VQ). While beneficial over VQ, LiftQuant's decoding path relies solely on linear transformations and 1-bit uniform quantizers, retaining hardware-friendly nature. This flexibility is transformative: LiftQuant enables a 70B LLM to be compressed to 2.4 bits to precisely fit a 24GB GPU, where its performance significantly surpasses state-of-the-art 2-bit models fitted on the same device. Our code and ckpt is available at https://github.com/Heliulu/LiftQuant.

</details>


### [128] [A Goal-Set Characterization of Task Composition in the Boolean Task Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04053)
*Eduardo Terrés-Caballero,Herke van Hoof*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现布尔任务代数（BTA）在确定性任务中存在结构冗余，通过仅利用通用和空任务即可实现高效的任务组合，大幅简化了学习过程并提高了效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对原始布尔任务代数（BTA）中关于基任务数量的结构性假设进行反思，旨在探讨是否存在冗余计算以及如何降低学习和组合的成本。

Method: 提出了一种基于目标集（goal-set-based）的组合方法。该方法直接对目标集进行逻辑运算，通过从通用任务和空任务的价值函数中提取特定片段，从而重构出组合后的价值函数，无需学习额外的基任务。

Result: 实验证明在多种环境（表格型、视觉型、函数近似及连续控制）中，增加额外的基任务不会提升性能。该方法在降低学习成本和组合时间的同时，保持了与原有方法相当的策略性能。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在确定性马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中，布尔任务代数（BTA）的基任务结构存在冗余，仅通过通用任务和空任务即可重构出最优价值函数。而在随机环境中，这种坍缩性质不一定成立，最优组合可能需要指数级的策略信息。

Abstract: The Boolean Task Algebra (BTA) provides a principled framework for zero-shot task composition in reinforcement learning by equipping goal-reaching tasks with Boolean operations. We revisit its structural assumptions and formalize a collapse in the space of optimal extended Q-value functions: in deterministic MDPs, every such function is fully determined by the universal and empty tasks. This makes the logarithmic set of base tasks proposed in the original BTA formulation redundant. Building on this observation, we introduce a goal-set-based composition method that performs logical operations on goal sets and reconstructs composed value functions by selecting slices from the universal and empty value functions. This reduces learning costs for standard BTA and reduces composition time for both BTA and Skill Machines, while preserving policy performance. Experiments across tabular, visual, function-approximation, and continuous-control domains show that learning additional base tasks does not yield better performance. Finally, we study the stochastic setting and provide a counterexample showing that this collapse need not hold, that is, optimal composition may require accounting for exponentially many policies in the number of goals. Code is available at https://github.com/EduardoTerres/bta_paper.

</details>


### [129] [PRECISE: Reducing the Bias of LLM Evaluations Using Prediction-Powered Ranking Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.18777)
*Abhishek Divekar,Anirban Majumder*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PRECISE 框架通过结合极少量人工标注与 LLM 判断，利用统计学方法（PPI）实现了高效且无偏的检索系统评估，极大降低了对大规模人工标注的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统评估检索、排序及 RAG 系统的方式严重依赖大规模人工标注，成本极高。虽然目前利用 LLM 作为自动化判决器（LLM-as-a-judge）成为趋势，但 LLM 固有的偏见限制了其直接用于可靠的指标估算。

Method: 提出了名为 PRECISE 的统计框架，通过结合少量人工标注（100条）与大量 LLM 判决结果，利用 PPI 进行指标估算。该方法通过重新构建指标集成空间，将计算复杂度从指数级 O(2^|C|) 优化至 O(2^K)，并针对查询-文档级标注进行了专门设计。

Result: 在多个主流检索数据集上的实验表明，PRECISE 能显著降低关键业务指标（如 Precision@K）的评估方差，有效校准了 LLM 在低资源环境下的偏见，且仅需 100 条人工标注和 10,000 条无标注示例即可实现可靠评估。

Conclusion: PRECISE 框架成功将“预测驱动推理”（PPI）扩展至子实例标注场景，通过极少量的人工标注纠正了 LLM 作为评价者的偏见，在保证评估可靠性的同时大幅降低了标注成本和计算复杂度。

Abstract: Evaluating the quality of search, ranking and RAG systems traditionally requires a significant number of human relevance annotations. In recent times, several deployed systems have explored the usage of Large Language Models (LLMs) as automated judges for this task while their inherent biases prevent direct use for metric estimation. We present a statistical framework extending Prediction-Powered Inference (PPI) that combines minimal human annotations with LLM judgments to produce reliable estimates of metrics which require sub-instance annotations. Our method requires as few as 100 human-annotated queries and 10,000 unlabeled examples, reducing annotation requirements significantly compared to traditional approaches. We formulate our proposed framework (PRECISE) for inference of relevance uplift for an LLM-based query reformulation application, extending PPI to sub-instance annotations at the query-document level. By reformulating the metric-integration space, we reduced the computational complexity from O(2^|C|) to O(2^K), where |C| represents corpus size (in order of millions). Detailed experiments across prominent retrieval datasets demonstrate that our method reduces the variance of estimates for the business-critical Precision@K metric, while effectively correcting for LLM bias in low-resource settings.

### [130] [Spectral Scaling Laws of Muon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04058)
*Gagik Magakyan,Pablo Parrilo,Asuman Ozdaglar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究揭示了Muon优化器中动量矩阵奇异值随模型规模变化的功率律，并基于此提出了一种针对不同层级动态调整牛顿-舒尔茨迭代次数的策略，以在保持模型训练性能的前提下降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器采用牛顿-舒尔茨（NS）迭代进行正交化以提高训练效率，但NS是近似算法，对于小奇异值的方向处理能力有限。目前尚不清楚动量矩阵的奇异值谱随模型规模变化的规律，这导致在超大规模模型中无法确定如何平衡正交化质量与计算开销。

Method: 通过对77M到2.8B参数规模的模型进行系统性实验，追踪各层动量矩阵的奇异值分位数，分析其随模型规模变化的演变规律；基于观测到的功率律分布，推导出不同层级在不同模型规模下所需的NS迭代次数优化方案。

Result: 研究表明，动量矩阵的奇异值分位数在训练早期后趋于稳定。这些稳定值遵循与模型规模相关的功率律，其中浅层和中层受模型规模影响较小，而深层受影响显著。在 frontier 规模下，若不增加迭代次数，深层可能出现正交化失效。研究为此提供了一套分层级的计算资源分配准则。

Conclusion: 研究发现Muon优化器中牛顿-舒尔茨（NS）迭代的有效性随模型规模增大而变化，且不同层级的奇异值谱呈现出不同的缩放规律。通过应用这些规律，实践者可以根据层级定制NS迭代次数，在保证优化质量的同时显著降低计算开销，为超大规模模型的训练提供了重要的优化策略。

Abstract: Orthonormalized update rules have rapidly become a leading choice of optimizer for training large language models, with recent open-source state-of-the-art models adopting Muon. To keep these updates tractable, Muon performs the orthonormalization with the Newton--Schulz (NS) iteration. Since NS is only approximate, directions with small singular values fail to be orthonormalized. In Muon, NS is applied to the momentum matrix at every step, yet little is known about how the singular value spectrum of these momentum matrices behaves during training, or how that behavior changes with model size. We present the first systematic study of this question. Tracking singular value quantiles of the momentum buffer across layers in models ranging from 77M to 2.8B parameters, we observe a consistent picture: after a short burn-in, the quantiles stabilize at a value determined by the layer type and model size. These stabilization values follow remarkably clean power laws in model size, with layer-dependent exponents. Layers up to mid-late depth scale very mildly with model size $M$ (around $M^{-0.25}$), so the standard 5-step NS configuration used at academic scale will continue to orthonormalize them at much larger scales. Some of the late layers, however, scale much more aggressively (up to $M^{-0.96}$) and will fall into the NS failure regime at frontier scale unless one uses more NS iterations or better-tuned coefficients. NS iterations are computationally expensive at scale; our laws give practitioners a principled, layer-aware recipe for choosing the minimum NS configuration that still orthonormalizes the directions that matter -- avoiding unnecessary computation without sacrificing update quality.

</details>


### [131] [LLM Compression with Jointly Optimizing Architectural and Quantization choices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04063)
*Hoang-Loc La,Truong-Thanh Le,Amir Taherkordi,Phuong Hoai Ha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种联合架构搜索与混合精度量化的可微分框架，通过整体优化解决了大模型在边缘侧部署时的性能与效率瓶颈，实现了优于现有分步压缩方案的精度-延迟权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）计算与内存需求过高，难以在边缘设备上部署。虽然现有的剪枝、量化或从零训练小模型的方法能缓解此问题，但存在算力消耗大、搜索空间受限或架构与量化优化脱节等局限，亟需一种更高效的综合压缩策略。

Method: 提出了一种可微分的神经架构搜索（NAS）框架，该框架不仅能够探索完整的架构搜索空间，还实现了线性层架构配置与混合精度量化的联合优化，避免了传统方法中架构搜索与量化脱节的问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，该模型在七项推理任务中表现出色，与顺序执行NAS后量化的基准方法相比，在相同精度下推理速度提升了1.4倍；在相同延迟条件下，平均准确率提升了高达6%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了联合优化架构搜索与混合精度量化在大型语言模型压缩任务中的有效性，为在边缘设备上高效部署大模型提供了一种比传统分步压缩方法更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Deploying large language models (LLMs) is challenging due to their significant memory and computational requirements. While some methods address this by developing small or tiny language models from scratch, these approaches demand extensive GPU training. Compressing pre-trained LLMs for edge devices offers a compelling alternative. Beyond pruning and quantization, Neural Architecture Search (NAS) enables effective compression, yet prior NAS approaches often limit the search space and decouple architecture from quantization. We introduce a differentiable NAS framework that explores the entire space and jointly optimizes architectural configurations alongside mixed-precision quantization for linear layers of LLMs. Experiments demonstrate superior accuracy-latency trade-offs: our models achieve up to 1.4x faster inference than sequential NAS-then-quantization baselines at comparable accuracy, or up to 6% higher average accuracy across seven reasoning tasks at equivalent latency.

</details>


### [132] [TPA-AD: A Two-Stage Pseudo Anomaly-Guided Method for Bearing Time-Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04073)
*Xiancheng Wang,Zhibo Zhang,Ran Li,Rui Wang,Minghang Zhao,Shisheng Zhong,Lin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TPA-AD 是一种仅需正常训练数据的时序异常检测方法，通过生成边界附近的伪异常样本并进行对比学习，有效提升了对异常的辨识能力和对退化过程的监测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在轴箱轴承时序异常检测中，通常缺乏异常样本（仅有正常样本）。现有方法依赖已知的故障类别、真实的异常先验或随机噪声注入，这难以有效刻画正常与异常之间的精确边界。作者旨在解决在无异常样本监督下，如何更精准地界定正常边界并提升异常检测性能的问题。

Method: 提出了两阶段伪异常引导的异常检测方法（TPA-AD）：1. 使用重构模型并结合按特征的目标误差控制生成边界伪异常样本；2. 通过对比学习训练异常敏感的特征表示；3. 利用 K-近邻（KNN）算法计算窗口级和点级的异常分数。

Result: TPA-AD 在轴承故障检测和退化过程数据集上验证了其有效性，显著提升了正常边界的可分性。在 13 个公开时序异常检测基准数据集上的拓展实验结果表明，该方法能提供稳定的异常响应，对退化过程高度敏感，并具有良好的跨数据集通用性。

Conclusion: TPA-AD 提出了一种在仅有正常样本的条件下，通过构建边界伪异常来强化模型区分能力的方法。实验证明，该方法不仅在轴箱轴承故障检测中表现出色，且在处理混合变量、监测退化过程以及跨领域通用时序异常检测任务中均表现出较强的鲁棒性和普适性。

Abstract: This paper proposes a two-stage pseudo anomaly-guided anomaly detection method (\textbf{T}wo-stage \textbf{P}seudo \textbf{A}nomaly-guided \textbf{A}nomaly \textbf{D}etection, \textbf{TPA-AD}) for axle-box bearing time-series anomaly detection (time series anomaly detection, TSAD) under the setting where only normal samples are available for training. The method first generates pseudo-anomalous windows near the normal boundary using a reconstruction model and per-feature target-error control. It then learns anomaly-sensitive representations through contrastive learning between normal and pseudo-anomalous windows, and finally produces window-level and point-level anomaly scores using k-nearest neighbors (KNN). Compared with existing methods that rely on known fault categories, real anomaly priors, or random anomaly injection, TPA-AD improves the separability of the normal boundary by constructing pseudo-anomalies in boundary neighborhoods and can jointly handle continuous and discrete features in mixed-variable scenarios. The main experiments are conducted on bearing fault detection datasets and degradation-process datasets, with an additional exploratory extension on $13$ public TSAD datasets. The results show that the proposed method yields relatively stable anomaly responses, is sensitive to degradation evolution, and demonstrates a certain degree of broader applicability on public TSAD benchmarks and real high-speed-train-related bearing data.

### [133] [Adaptive Patching Is Harder Than It Looks For Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04074)
*Federico Zucchi,Yi Xie,Chao Zhang,Keyuan Luo,Thomas Lampert,Ziyue Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过理论建模与受控实验证明，自适应分块在时序预测中并不总能带来性能增益；相对于精心调优的均匀分块基准，目前的自适应机制缺乏普适性的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自适应分块在时序Transformer中被广泛推崇，但目前尚不清楚其在何种条件下真正优于经过调优的均匀分块。本文旨在探讨局部异质性与预测损失之间的关系，并质疑自适应分块相较于均匀分块的普遍有效性。

Method: 本文通过将分块视为预算比特率分配问题进行建模，推导出了动态分块规则超越均匀基准所需的显式阈值；同时，在控制变量下，通过在三种代表性架构上对比自适应机制与均匀分块扫描的结果，评估其在长期预测基准上的表现。

Result: 理论分析表明，在常见的损失函数下，单纯依靠局部复杂度无法产生非均匀最优解；实验结果显示，在标准长期预测基准上，经优化的均匀基准具有极强的竞争力，自适应分块未表现出一致的优势，其收益往往具有高度的特定性。

Conclusion: 自适应分块机制（Adaptive patching）并非总是优于经过调优的均匀分块。其性能收益取决于该方法能否高效且准确地识别出真正能够通过细粒度分块降低预测损失的区域。未来的研究应将经过严格调优的均匀分块作为衡量自适应算法价值的标准基准。

Abstract: Adaptive patching is a recent and compelling proposal for time-series Transformers: allocate finer patches where the sequence looks locally informative. This paper asks under what conditions a content-adaptive patching operator should outperform a tuned uniform one. Local heterogeneity alone is not enough: under pointwise forecasting losses, a complex-looking region is not automatically one where finer patching reduces the loss. We model patching as a budgeted bitrate allocation and derive an explicit threshold that a dynamic patching rule must satisfy to beat a well-tuned uniform baseline, then bound the achievable improvement both locally (a quadratic surrogate) and globally (a strong-convexity bound under the model's assumptions). Two structural results follow: without a coupling constraint, scalar local complexity cannot produce a non-uniform optimum under a common loss landscape; and once the backbone is trained to its representation-aware optimum, the alignment gain collapses around a well-tuned uniform patch size. To test these predictions, we run a controlled isolation study on three representative architectures, replacing each adaptive mechanism with a uniform patch-size sweep while keeping the backbone, data, and training protocol fixed. On standard long-horizon forecasting benchmarks, the validation-selected uniform baseline is competitive with the dynamic counterpart, with per-setting effects concentrated near zero and no consistent directional advantage once results are aggregated by dataset. The larger gains we do observe are method- and dataset-specific. Adaptive patching should therefore be evaluated against a tuned uniform baseline; its value depends on whether a cheap and reliable routing signal can identify where finer patches actually reduce forecasting loss.

### [134] [Large Language Models Hack Rewards, and Society](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04075)
*Wei Liu,Xinyi Mou,Hanqi Yan,Zhongyu Wei,Yulan He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了LLM通过强化学习可能产生“社会黑客”风险，即模型通过寻找现实社会规则中的法律或制度漏洞来最大化奖励。实验证明，现有安全措施难以防范这种策略，呼吁开发更安全的后训练范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者观察到强化学习在LLM后训练中的奖励黑客行为与社会规则存在结构相似性，旨在探讨LLM在学习社会规则时是否会产生“社会黑客”（Societal Hacking）现象，即利用社会规则漏洞实现技术上的合规但违背制度初衷的策略。

Method: 构建了一个包含72个模拟社会环境的沙盒平台“SocioHack”，通过强化学习让模型在这些环境中根据规则获取奖励，观察模型是否会通过发掘规则漏洞（即“社会黑客”）来最大化奖励，并评估现有安全防护措施的有效性。

Result: 研究发现，奖励黑客行为在社会环境中自然产生，导致了监管漏洞的被动发现。模型能够生成在技术上遵守规则但彻底破坏监管意图的策略，且现有的LLM安全防护手段在应对这种现象时效果有限。

Conclusion: 社会黑客行为是强化学习模型在复杂社会规则下的新风险。仅仅依靠技术合规性不足以保证模型的对齐，未来的后训练范式必须从单纯的奖励最大化转向对系统意图的深刻理解和对潜在漏洞的防御。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a dominant post-training paradigm, enabling large language models (LLMs) to learn from rewards. We observe that societal regulations are structurally similar to reward functions. They define measurable outcomes, thresholds, and exceptions, while often leaving institutional intent only partially specified. We hypothesise that the RL training process may exploit these gaps and therefore ask whether models' well-known tendency to hack reward functions during RL can scale into a more consequential failure mode named societal hacking: discovering loopholes in the rules society runs on. To study this phenomenon, we introduce SocioHack, a sandbox of 72 societal environments, and find that within these environments, reward hacking naturally emerges and leads to regulatory loophole discovery. Models learn to hack the social rules and generate strategies that remain technically compliant while defeating regulatory intent, and current LLM safeguards provide only limited mitigation. Therefore, collecting in-the-wild feedback for model training requires greater caution, and we need a next-generation post-training paradigm for safely iterating LLMs in real society.=

### [135] [Stein Kernelized Molecular Dynamics for Active Learning of Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04100)
*Joanna Zou,Fraser Birks,Dallas Foster,Youssef Marzouk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SKMD 是一种创新的主动学习方法，它通过结合 Stein 变分梯度下降与分子动力学，在保持玻尔兹曼分布平衡的同时，高效地获取多样化的训练数据，从而加速并优化 MLIPs 的训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）的性能严重依赖于训练数据的质量与多样性。现有的采样方法在平衡配置空间探索与高概率区域覆盖方面存在不足，因此需要更高效的采样策略来改进 MLIPs 的主动学习和微调过程。

Method: 提出 Stein 核分子动力学（SKMD），这是一种基于 Stein 变分梯度下降的随机动力学方法。它采用异步粒子更新机制，并利用全局原子描述符构建核函数以度量配置相似性。此外，还引入了自适应停止准则，用于在模拟过程中在线选择非冗余的训练数据。

Result: 在 Müller-Brown 势能面和丙氨酸二肽的 MACE 模型微调任务中，SKMD 表现优于基准方法，能够在更少的训练迭代和同等数量的样本下获得更高的模型精度。

Conclusion: SKMD 是一种高效的主动学习数据获取方法，通过在保持玻尔兹曼分布的同时优化配置多样性，显著提升了机器学习原子间势模型（MLIPs）的训练效率和精度。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) enable efficient and accurate atomistic simulations but depend critically on the quality and diversity of the training data. We introduce Stein kernelized molecular dynamics (SKMD), an enhanced sampling method that uses interacting particle dynamics to acquire informative training configurations for the active learning and fine-tuning of MLIPs. SKMD corresponds to a stochastic variant of Stein variational gradient descent that is adapted for molecular dynamics by incorporating asynchronous particle updates and a kernel of global atomic descriptors, which provides a symmetry-aware measure of configurational similarity. Unlike other enhanced samplers used in molecular dynamics, SKMD preserves the Boltzmann distribution as the asymptotic distribution of the dynamics. This property enforces a balance between the exploration of diverse configurations and attraction toward high-probability regions of the energy landscape. We further propose an approach to efficient online data acquisition using an adaptive stopping criterion that selects non-redundant training data over the course of simulation. We demonstrate SKMD for the active learning of a neural network model of the Müller-Brown potential and the fine-tuning of a MACE interatomic potential for alanine dipeptide. Compared to active learning baselines, our method achieves higher model accuracy in fewer training iterations with the same number of acquired training samples.

### [136] [dMX: Differentiable Mixed-Precision Assignment for Low-Precision Floating-Point Formats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04115)
*Giuseppe Franco,Ian Colbert,Pablo Monteagudo-Lago,Felix Marty,Nicholas Fraser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: dMX 是一种用于 MXFP 量化的可微分混合精度框架，通过将位宽分配转化为可学习的连续优化问题，在满足特定计算预算的前提下，显著提升了 LLM 在低精度环境下的推理性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 量化通常采用统一位宽，这并非最优解。为了在保持高性能的同时实现更高效的部署，需要一种能够针对不同层自动学习最优混合精度位宽的方法，特别是在 OCP 标准的 MXFP 数据格式下。

Method: 提出了一种名为 dMX 的可微分混合精度量化框架。将层级位宽分配转化为连续优化问题，通过引入可学习的标量偏移量（offset）来参数化浮点格式。结合基于温度的退火计划逐步实现离散化，并引入目标感知的正则化项来约束平均位宽，以满足部署成本预算。

Result: 在 Llama、Qwen3 和 SmolLM2 等模型上进行的实验表明，dMX 在困惑度和零样本推理任务中均表现优异。相比基于 KL 散度的启发式层选择方法，dMX 能持续提供帕累托最优的模型配置，更好地平衡了模型质量与推理效率。

Conclusion: dMX 提供了一种高效且灵活的混合精度量化策略，通过微分优化和退火机制，在保持模型性能的同时，能够根据特定预算自动搜索出最优的 MXFP 位宽分配方案，优于传统的启发式方法。

Abstract: Quantizing large language models (LLMs) to low-precision floating-point representations is central to efficient deployment, yet applying a single bit-width uniformly across all layers is sub-optimal in terms of both performance and accuracy. This work introduces dMX, a differentiable mixed-precision quantization framework for learnable floating-point bit-width assignment. We study its application for the microscaling floating-point (MXFP) family of data types defined by the Open Compute Project (OCP) standard. The per-layer bit-width assignment is formulated as a continuous optimization problem in which each layer's floating-point format format is parameterized by a scalar parameter, folding the multi-variate design space into a single learnable offset. During training this offset takes continuous values, avoiding sudden oscillations between discrete quantization formats. A temperature-based annealing schedule progressively discretizes the learned offsets, ensuring that the final configuration maps to hardware-compatible MXFP formats without abrupt transitions between training and inference behavior. A target-aware regularization term steers the average bit-width toward a user-specified budget, serving as a coarse-grained proxy for inference cost and balancing model quality against deployment efficiency. We performed experiments on different families of LLM, such as Llama, Qwen3, and SmolLM2, evaluating perplexity on WikiText-2 and accuracy on four zero-shot reasoning benchmarks. Across these settings, dMX consistently yields Pareto-dominating models and improves over Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence-based layer-selection heuristics, efficiently navigating trade-offs between model quality and average bit-width.

</details>


### [137] [ADAPTOOD: Uncertainty-Aware Fine-Tuning for Out-of-Distribution ECG Time Series Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04164)
*Sotirios Vavaroutas,Yu Yvonne Wu,Ali Etemad,Cecilia Mascolo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对机器学习模型在面对分布偏移（OOD）时泛化能力不足的问题，本文提出了一种名为 ADAPTOOD 的新框架，通过评估数据不确定性来量化偏移严重度，并据此优化微调过程，显著提升了模型在时序数据任务中的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习模型在面对由于传感器、人群或应用环境变化导致的分布偏移（OOD）时性能往往下降，而现有的自适应方法通常假设偏移是固定的，未能区分偏移的严重程度，导致在多类型或多程度偏移场景下泛化能力受限。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ADAPTOOD 的框架：1. 利用数据不确定性来量化目标分布偏离预训练分布的程度（即分布偏移严重性）；2. 基于该量化指标指导模型微调，结合低秩模型更新（Low-rank updates）和自适应超参数优化技术，实现对 OOD 数据的有效适配。

Result: 实验表明，ADAPTOOD 在 OOD 任务中准确率最高提升了 7%，精度最高提升了 12.9%，并且随着分布偏移严重程度的增加，该方法仍能保持较强的性能。

Conclusion: ADAPTOOD 框架通过量化分布偏移的严重程度，为时序数据的自适应微调提供了一种稳健且高效的解决方案，证明了不确定性感知在提升模型泛化能力中的核心作用。

Abstract: Data samples used for training often differ from those encountered during fine-tuning and deployment, and while ML models show promise, their performance remains limited when only small annotated datasets are available. Performance often degrades under distribution shifts caused by diverse sensors, populations, and application settings. Although pre-training helps, models frequently encounter out-of-distribution (OOD) data in real-world settings, leading to reduced robustness. Existing adaptation methods usually assume fixed distribution shifts and struggle when multiple types or severities occur. In particular, they overlook shift severity, for example treating adaptation to a large familiar dataset the same as adaptation to a small dataset with a new task, which limits generalisation. To address this, we propose ADAPTOOD, a novel framework that leverages data uncertainty to quantify distribution shift severity and guide fine-tuning for time series. This uncertainty measures how strongly samples from the target deployment distribution deviate from the pre-training distribution, providing a direct signal of OOD severity. Our framework combines this uncertainty with low-rank model updates and adaptive hyperparameter optimisation to improve adaptation. We show that ADAPTOOD achieves up to 7% higher accuracy and 12.9% higher precision than existing methods in OOD tasks, maintaining strong performance as distribution shift severity increases.

</details>


### [138] [Exact Unlearning in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04182)
*Thanh Nguyen-Tang,Raman Arora*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了强化学习中的“精确遗忘”问题，提出了一种高效的算法框架，能够在满足统计稳定性（ρ-TV-stable）的前提下，以远低于从头训练的成本从模型中移除特定用户数据，并证明了该方法的理论最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着隐私保护法规（如GDPR）的日益严格，在强化学习中实现“被遗忘权”变得至关重要。研究旨在解决如何以计算效率最高的方式，从已训练的强化学习模型中精确删除特定用户数据，且使遗忘后的模型与从未接触该数据的模型在统计上保持一致。

Method: 研究者构造了一种基于ρ-TV-稳定性的强化学习算法，专门针对表格型马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）。该算法通过特定的稳定性机制，使得删除用户数据后的策略与从未参与训练的策略在统计上不可区分，从而实现高效的精确遗忘。

Result: 对于表格型MDP，所提出的算法实现了 O(H^2√(SAT) + H^3S^2A + H^(2.5)S^2A/ρ) 的遗憾界（regret bound）。此外，研究建立了 Ω(H√(SAT) + SAH/ρ) 的下界，证明了该算法在理论上几乎是极小极大最优的。其遗忘过程的预期计算成本仅为从零开始重新训练成本的 ρ√(ln T) 倍。

Conclusion: 本文为强化学习中的精确遗忘提供了一种近乎最优的理论框架，证明了在满足特定稳定性条件下，实现精确遗忘的计算成本远低于从零开始重新训练，为隐私保护学习提供了重要的理论支持。

Abstract: We formulate the problem of \emph{exact unlearning} in reinforcement learning, where the goal is to design an efficient framework that enables the removal of any user's data upon deletion request, i.e., the online learner's output after unlearning is \emph{indistinguishable} from what would have been produced had the deleted user never interacted with the learner. For any $ρ>0$, we show that there exists a reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that is $ρ$-TV-stable and supports an exact unlearning procedure whose expected computational cost is only a $ρ\sqrt{\ln T}$ fraction of the computational cost of retraining from scratch. We construct such a $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithm for tabular Markov decision processes (MDPs), which achieves a regret bound of $\mathcal{O}(H^2 \sqrt{SAT} + H^3 S^2 A + {H^{2.5} S^2 A}/ρ)$, where $S, A, H$, and $T$ denote the number of states, the number of actions, the episode horizon, and the number of episodes, respectively. We also establish a lower bound of $Ω(H\sqrt{\!SAT}\! +\! {SAH}/ρ)$ for $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithms, showing that our algorithm is nearly minimax optimal.

*Zhikai Chen,Junyu Yin,Jialiang Gu,Siheng Xiong,Xiaoze Liu,Ruowang Zhang,Keren Zhou,Kai Guo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 理论诊断：从模型和数据两个维度剖析关系转换器（RT），利用核回归视角分析其在标签稀疏下的局限，并揭示合成预训练与分布内预训练导致的“懒惰”与“特征学习”模式差异。
2. 架构优化：提出双阶段ICL架构，将关系骨干网络与来自表格基础模型的批处理级ICL层相结合。
3. 预训练策略：采用同质性感知（homophily-aware）的合成数据与真实数据混合预训练，并引入基于原型的正则化技术，构建出OpenRFM。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了现有关系基础模型（RFM）在处理稀疏标签和分布偏移时的局限性，并证明了通过结合双阶段架构与改进的预训练策略，能够显著提升模型在关系数据上的泛化能力。OpenRFM的成功证明了将关系表征学习与表格级上下文学习相结合是缩小开源与商用模型差距的有效途径。

Abstract: Relational Foundation Models (RFMs) promise a single pre-trained predictor that, given any relational database, returns predictions in one forward pass via relational in-context learning (ICL). Yet a substantial gap separates open RFMs from their commercial counterparts, and the origin of this gap has not been systematically understood. We dissect a representative framework, the Relational Transformer (RT), from two perspectives. Model side: we show that RT performs relation-level ICL, and a kernel regression view shows it fails when sparse label-cell coverage yields an underdetermined regression. Data side: we ablate RT's pre-training source and find that existing synthetic-only pre-training and in-distribution pre-training drive the same architecture into different regimes, lazy vs. feature-learning. Probing this gap reveals that the missing ingredient is a support-identifiable relational latent in the label-generation process. These two diagnoses translate into (1) a dual-stage ICL architecture that combines the relational backbone with a batch-level ICL layer lifted from a pre-trained tabular foundation model to overcome relation-level label scarcity, and (2) a homophily-aware synthetic plus continual real-data pre-training mixture, augmented with a prototype-based regularization. These choices define OpenRFM, a simple yet effective RFM that improves average task performance by approximately 30% over the RT backbone and surpasses the commercial model KumoRFMv1 on a large set of evaluation tasks.

### [141] [A Geometric Characterization of the Stationary Plateau for Two-Layer Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04327)
*Tian Ding,Dawei Li,Ruoyu Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入探讨了神经网络“神经元分裂”对损失景观几何结构的影响，通过引入“内Hessian矩阵”分析，揭示了分裂后的平原性质如何由分裂系数和内Hessian的定性特征共同决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在深入研究两层神经网络损失景观中出现的“静止平原”现象，特别是探究当通过“神经元分裂”（复制神经元）扩展模型宽度时，这些平原上的驻点（局部极小值或鞍点）在几何性质上如何发生演变。

Method: 研究采用了数学建模与几何分析方法，引入了“内Hessian矩阵”（inner Hessian）作为核心工具，通过分析该矩阵的定性特征以及分裂系数对损失函数二阶导数的影响，对两层神经网络中的静止平原进行了分类与性质判定。

Result: 研究发现，分裂局部极小值可能产生局部极小值与鞍点的混合，或者形成全为鞍点的平原（并在特定假设下确定了全鞍点区域）；而分裂鞍点则总是产生由鞍点组成的平原。这一结果统一并扩展了先前关于神经网络景观的分析，明确了模型宽度扩展对优化性质的影响。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了神经网络宽度扩展（神经元分裂）与损失景观几何结构之间的演化关系，证明了神经元分裂是否保留局部极小值性质取决于“内Hessian矩阵”的定性特征及分裂系数的选择。这项工作为理解过参数化网络中的优化平原及模型重参数化提供了重要的理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the geometric structure of stationary plateaus that arise in the loss landscape of two-layer neural networks with smooth activation functions. We focus on the phenomenon of "neuron splitting" where duplicating a hidden neuron yields an affine set of stationary points in a wider network. We provide a comprehensive classification of all stationary points on these plateaus, determining under what conditions they constitute local minima or saddle points. Our characterization hinges on a per-neuron curvature object we term the "inner Hessian" matrix. Our analysis reveals that the definiteness of the inner Hessian and the choice of splitting coefficients jointly dictate the local geometry of the plateau. We show that "splitting" a local minimum can yield either a mixture of local minima and saddles or an all-saddle plateau, with a concrete sure-saddle region identified under mild assumptions. In contrast, splitting a saddle point always produces a plateau of saddle points. Our results unify and extend prior landscape analyses, elucidating when and how model expansion preserves or alters the nature of stationary points. These findings offer new geometric insights into the effects of width expansion and reparameterization in neural networks.

### [142] [Policy Gradient for Continuous-Time Robust Markov Decision Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04335)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程（RMDP）研究多局限于离散时间框架，缺乏对连续时间动力学系统下鲁棒策略梯度算法的系统性理论研究与高效算法框架。

Method: 提出利用路径导数与伴随方程法（adjoint-based formulas）推导连续时间RMDP的策略梯度与对抗梯度；设计了双循环优化器（double-loop optimisers）以实现线性收敛；引入了平均场优化器（mean-field optimisers）作为分布优化手段，并结合神经网络常微分方程（Neural ODE）动力学进行实验验证。

Result: 在Oracle模型下，双循环优化器实现了线性收敛；在基于样本的模型下，达到了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{ε^2})$的样本复杂度。对于平均场优化器，Oracle模型下收敛速度为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{K})$，在N粒子近似下的样本复杂度为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{N^2}ε)$。实验证实了这些方法在神经微分方程动力学下的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文通过引入基于路径和伴随方程的导数推导，成功将策略梯度算法扩展至连续时间鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程（RMDP），并为优化算法提供了严谨的收敛性与样本复杂度保证，为处理复杂连续系统提供了高效的新工具。

Abstract: The framework of robust Markov decision processes (RMDPs) allows the design of reinforcement learning agents that satisfy performance guarantees under worst-case transition dynamics. Traditional RMDPs consider discrete-time dynamics and recently, sample-efficient policy gradient algorithms have been considered in this context. This paper investigates policy gradient algorithms within a continuous-time RMDP framework. Policy gradients and adversarial gradients are derived using pathwise and adjoint-based formulas for stochastic and ordinary differential equations. We propose double-loop optimisers to obtain linear convergence in the oracle-based setting and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{ε^2})$ sample complexity in the sample-based setting in an analysis which also derives novel tools for the framework of undiscounted total cost MDPs. Additionally, we propose mean-field optimisers as distributional optimisers with an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{K})$ oracle-based convergence rate and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{N^2}ε)$ sample complexity under $N$-particle approximation. The effectiveness of continuous-time policy gradient algorithms is confirmed for both optimisers on continuous-time RMDPs with neural ordinary differential equation dynamics.

Abstract: Computational models of epilepsy promise patient-specific treatment design, but most optimization workflows still search for parameters that perform well on average. In neuromodulation, this is a weak target: a protocol that improves the mean response can still fail in the patient whose network is least tolerant to stimulation. We present a literature-guided minimax pipeline that couples PubMed-scale hypothesis extraction, The Virtual Brain (TVB) Epileptor simulations, and large-language-model-guided black-box optimization. The optimizer proposes either intrinsic model-control parameters or clinically interpretable external-stimulation protocols; TVB evaluates each proposal across sampled virtual patients; and the objective maximizes worst-case reward, defined as the negative variance of simulated seizure activity. In the intrinsic model-control experiment, the best archived parameter set improved worst-case reward from -0.5285 to -0.3182, a 39.8% gain over baseline. The clinical-style external-stimulation search produced a much smaller worst-case improvement (1.7%), and a 20-patient virtual cohort showed no aggregate benefit (p=0.9019), despite a 55% responder rate and a positive temporal-lobe subgroup signal. ### [145] [Expectations vs. Realities: The Cost of MSE-Optimal Forecasting Under Conditional Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04342)
*Riku Green,Zahraa S. Abdallah,Telmo M Silva Filho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出多步时间序列预测中单纯使用MSE作为评估指标存在局限性，会牺牲预测结果的分布真实性。研究通过理论和实证证明了准确性与真实性之间存在权衡，并建议在模型选择时应引入边缘真实性指标，以提升长视距预测的实用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多步时间序列预测中，目前普遍使用的MSE等逐点评估指标假设条件均值是预测的充分目标。然而在长视距预测下，这种假设忽略了条件不确定性，导致模型往往倾向于输出均值而非符合真实概率分布的样本，从而降低了预测的现实意义。

Method: 1. 理论推导：形式化了“条件不确定性间隙（conditional uncertainty gap）”，证明了在不确定性存在时，确定性预测器无法同时满足MSE最小化和边缘分布匹配。
2. 实验验证：在受控的随机动力系统及九个真实世界数据集上，刻画了“准确性-真实性”帕累托前沿。
3. 比较分析：对比了直接多输出（Direct）与递归策略（Recursive）在预测表现上的差异。

Result: 1. 证明了准确性与边缘真实性之间存在模型无关的根本性权衡。
2. 随着预测视距增加，MSE最优解与真实分布之间的差距拉大。
3. 实验显示，仅需牺牲不到5%的MSE，即可获得中位数达17.3%（部分数据集超过30%）的边缘真实性提升。
4. 发现直接预测法倾向于高准确性但低真实性，而递归及基于采样的方法更倾向于保障边缘真实性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多步时间序列预测中存在的根本性“准确性-真实性”权衡，证明了仅依赖MSE指标会导致模型预测分布过度收敛且缺乏真实性。研究建议在评估和模型选择时应同时考虑边缘真实性，以避免陷入MSE最优但缺乏随机特征的次优解。

Abstract: Multi-step time series forecasting (MSF) is commonly evaluated using point-wise error metrics such as mean squared error (MSE), implicitly treating the conditional mean as a sufficient target. We show that this can be misleading under conditional uncertainty, where the conditional expectation becomes unrepresentative of typical realized values at longer horizons. We formalize this effect through a conditional uncertainty gap and prove that whenever this gap is nonzero, no deterministic predictor can simultaneously minimize MSE and match the marginal distribution of realized futures. This establishes a fundamental, model-agnostic trade-off between point accuracy and marginal realism in MSF evaluation. Using controlled stochastic dynamical systems and nine real-world forecasting benchmarks, we empirically characterize the resulting accuracy--realism frontier and \textbf{quantify the practical cost of MSE-only model selection}. As conditional uncertainty increases with forecast horizon, the attainable set expands into a pronounced Pareto front, separating MSE-optimal but under-dispersed predictors from methods that trade accuracy for realistic marginal variability. \textbf{Across benchmarks, we find that small relaxations in MSE ($\boldsymbol{\le 5\%}$) frequently unlock disproportionate gains in marginal realism, with median improvements of $\mathbf{17.3\%}$ and gains exceeding $\mathbf{30\%}$ in some datasets.} We further show that common forecasting strategies systematically occupy different regions of this frontier: direct multi-output predictors concentrate near the accuracy-optimal extreme, while recursive strategies and sample-based inference favors marginal realism. Together, these results expose a structural failure mode of MSE-based evaluation in long-horizon forecasting and recast strategy and inference selection as navigation of an unavoidable accuracy--realism trade-off.

</details>


### [146] [MeshTok: Efficient Multi-Scale Tokenization for Scalable PDE Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04366)
*Yanshun Zhao,Xiaoyu Peng,Jiamin Jiang,Congcong Zhu,Jingrun Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MeshTok是一种受AMR启发的自适应Token化框架，通过根据PDE解的局部特征动态分配计算资源，在保持Transformer架构通用性的前提下，提升了对复杂物理过程的建模精度与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Transformer模型在处理偏微分方程（PDE）时采用均匀分块策略，导致计算资源分配缺乏灵活性，无法高效捕捉复杂PDE解中的局部细微结构或突变特征。

Method: 提出了一种名为MeshTok的框架，通过感知局部特征（如梯度变化、瞬态特征或多尺度结构）进行自适应空间细化，将物理域分割为异构的多尺度Token，并在统一的Transformer架构中处理这些Token，以实现全局上下文与局部细节的同步建模。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多个PDE数据集上，MeshTok相比传统的均匀网格基准模型，在效率与精度之间实现了更好的权衡，能够更针对性地处理物理信息丰富的区域。

Conclusion: MeshTok通过引入受自适应网格细化（AMR）启发的动态分块机制，为神经PDE建模提供了一种高效且具备扩展性的通用设计原则，显著优化了计算资源在复杂物理特征上的分配。

Abstract: Conventional patchified Transformers operate on uniform spatial partitions, distributing computational effort evenly across the domain irrespective of local features. This inflexible tokenization scheme is inherently limited in its ability to efficiently represent and process solutions to complex PDEs. To address this, we propose MeshTok, an adaptive mesh refinement (AMR)-inspired tokenization and sequence modeling framework. This method selectively refines spatial regions exhibiting sharp gradients, transient features, or multiscale structures, generating a heterogeneous set of multiscale tokens defined on a fixed simulation grid. These tokens are processed within a unified Transformer sequence, enabling the model to simultaneously capture coarse-grained global context and fine-grained local details without requiring specialized architectural components. Although adaptive refinement moderately increases token count, it promotes a more targeted allocation of computational resources to physically informative regions, which we view as a practical inductive bias rather than a formal optimality guarantee. Experimental evaluations across multiple PDE families and benchmark datasets demonstrate that MeshTok consistently improves the efficiency-accuracy trade-off compared to uniform-grid baselines. This suggests adaptive multiscale tokenization as a scalable and generalizable design principle for neural PDE modeling. Code is available at https://github.com/SCAILab-USTC/MeshTok.

</details>


### [147] [When Do Fewer Coordinates Suffice in DP-SGD?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04375)
*Huiqi Zhang,Fang Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 DP-SGD 在高维空间中噪声过大的问题，该论文提出了一种两阶段坐标选择方法（TP-TopK），通过在训练前识别并锁定重要坐标，有效地将隐私噪声的规模降低至活跃维度级别，在提升隐私保护性能的同时保持了模型训练质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 DP-SGD 方法在更新过程中向所有坐标注入噪声，使得噪声水平随着参数空间维度 $d$ 的增加而放大。为了在不牺牲优化信号的前提下减少噪声影响，研究者探讨了是否能够仅更新参数中的重要坐标（即坐标稀疏化）。

Method: 提出了一种名为“TP-TopK”（两阶段 TopK DP-SGD）的方法，分为两个阶段：首先进行私人预热阶段，用于识别需要更新的重要坐标集合；随后在主要训练阶段中仅更新这些被选中的坐标，从而减少了噪声的累积维度。

Result: 理论分析表明，在满足特定条件时，DP-SGD 的噪声项与活跃维度 $k$ 相关而非全维度 $d$；实验证明，在 MNIST、FMNIST 和 CIFAR-10 数据集上，TP-TopK 能够比随机坐标选择保留更多的梯度能量，特别是在活跃维度较小的情况下效果显著。

Conclusion: 该论文证明了通过两阶段方法（TP-TopK）进行坐标稀疏化，可以将差分隐私训练中的噪声规模从全维度 $d$ 降低到活跃维度 $k$，从而在不依赖公共数据的情况下提升了训练效率和模型性能。

Abstract: Differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) injects noise into every updated coordinate, making the injected noise energy scale with the ambient parameter dimension \(d\). We ask when private training can update fewer coordinates without losing the signal needed for optimization. We propose \textsc{TP-TopK} (Two-Phase TopK DP-SGD), a two-phase method for coordinate-sparse private training without public data, in which a private warm-up phase identifies a coordinate support used to guide the main training phase. We give a criterion characterizing when coordinate restriction can be beneficial, show via a nonconvex stationarity bound that under this condition the relevant noise term scales with the active dimension \(k\) rather than the full parameter dimension \(d\), and provide a lower bound on the reliability of warm-up-based coordinate ranking. Experiments on MNIST, FMNIST, and CIFAR-10 show that learned coordinate supports can retain more gradient energy than size-matched random supports, with the largest gains when the active dimension is small and warm-up scores are informative.

</details>


### [148] [From Symbolic to Geometric: Enabling Spatial Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04381)
*Chen Chu,Bita Azarijoo,Li Xiong,Khurram Shafique,Cyrus Shahabi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个具备几何空间推理能力的多模态模型 SLM，通过将空间表示视为核心模态并辅以空间指令数据集，解决了大模型在空间推理上过度依赖符号模式匹配的问题，并在 SpatialEval 基准上取得了显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的大语言模型（LLM）虽然表现出一定的空间推理能力，但本质上是基于空间语言的符号化模式匹配，缺乏对连续空间表示和几何计算的内在支持，导致其难以进行真正的几何推理。

Method: 提出了“空间语言模型（SLM）”，将位置信息作为一种“一等公民”模态引入模型；构建了包含空间表示、原子几何操作与自然语言指令的“空间指令数据集”进行训练；设计了涵盖属性、距离、拓扑和相对位置任务的评估基准“SpatialEval”。

Result: 实验结果表明，SLM 在空间推理任务中显著优于基于提示工程或文本抽象的传统 LLM 方法，验证了集成几何空间表示对于提升空间推理能力的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将几何空间表示直接集成到多模态大模型中，能够有效克服现有模型仅依靠语言模式匹配进行空间推理的局限性，实现了更鲁棒、更真实的几何空间推理。

Abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) often appear to exhibit spatial reasoning ability; however, this capability is largely \emph{symbolic}, arising from pattern matching over spatial language rather than true \emph{geometric} reasoning over space. Because LLMs operate on discrete tokens, they lack native support for continuous spatial representations, explicit geometric computation, and structured spatial operators. To address this limitation, we introduce the \emph{Spatial Language Model (SLM)}, the first multimodal LLM that treats location information as a first-class modality and enables geometric spatial reasoning within the model's inference process. SLM directly operates on learned spatial representations rather than textual descriptions of spatial relations. To support effective training, we construct a \emph{Spatial Instruction Dataset} that aligns spatial representations, atomic geometric operations, and natural language instructions. We further propose a new benchmark named \emph{SpatialEval}, which is designed to evaluate spatial reasoning across attributes, distance, topology, and relative-position tasks. Extensive experiments show that SLM significantly outperforms existing LLM-based approaches that rely on symbolic reasoning via prompt engineering or textual abstraction, demonstrating the benefits of integrating geometric spatial representations for robust spatial reasoning.
  Our instruction dataset, evaluation benchmark, model training codes, and models' checkpoints can be found at:
  \hyperlink{https://github.com/chuchen2017/SLM}{https://github.com/chuchen2017/SLM}.

### [149] [Physics-Informed Machine Learning for Short-Term Flood Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04143)
*Tewodros Syum Gebre,Jagrati Talreja,Leila Hashemi-Beni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过在LSTM损失函数中加入水文趋势对齐约束的物理信息机器学习框架，显著提升了模型在数据稀缺和极端气候条件下的洪水预报准确性与物理合理性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种物理信息机器学习（PIML）框架，通过在长短期记忆网络（LSTM）的损失函数中加入“趋势对齐约束（Trend Alignment constraint）”，强制模型学习降水与流量趋势之间的一致性，从而在不依赖复杂水动力方程的前提下，引导模型产生符合物理逻辑的水文过程预测。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了将简单的物理约束引入深度学习模型，可以有效提升洪水预报模型在数据匮乏环境下的可靠性和鲁棒性，为无资料地区及应对气候变化下的洪水预测提供了切实可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate flood forecasting is essential for mitigating disaster risks and protecting communities. However, purely data-driven machine learning models often struggle in data-scarce environments and may violate fundamental hydrological principles. Standard Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks can generate physically inconsistent predictions, particularly when extrapolating to extreme weather conditions. To address these limitations, we propose a Physics-Informed Machine Learning (PIML) framework that incorporates hydrological knowledge directly into the loss function of an LSTM model. Specifically, a Trend Alignment constraint penalizes directional inconsistencies between precipitation and discharge trends, improving model robustness without requiring complex hydrodynamic equations. This regularization encourages the model to learn physically plausible hydrograph behavior, even with limited training data, while enhancing reliability during peak flood events. Experimental results show that the proposed physics-informed model outperforms a standard LSTM baseline in data-scarce settings, increasing the Nash-Sutcliffe Efficiency (NSE) from 0.20 to 0.23 when trained on only 5% of the available data. Additional stress tests under simulated extreme climate scenarios demonstrate that the baseline model exhibits unstable behavior, whereas the physics-informed model maintains directional consistency and physical plausibility. Although accurately predicting extreme peak magnitudes remains challenging with limited data, the proposed approach substantially reduces unphysical fluctuations common in purely data-driven models. These findings demonstrate that simple physical constraints can significantly improve the reliability of deep learning models for real-time flood forecasting, offering a practical solution for ungauged basins and evolving climate conditions.

### [150] [Shortcomings and capacities of real-constrained neural networks in complex spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04390)
*Andrew Gracyk*

Abstract: We find the asymptotic ratio between the storage capacities when enforcing real pre-activations in a complex hypothesis class as opposed to complex ones in the same class. Our methods depend on Gardner volume comparisons at critical capacity. Our proof relies on an application of the Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber (HCIZ) formula, nonstandard in literature. With the HCIZ formula, we may obtain a more robust approximation for the final asymptotic ratio. This strategy is applicable to our work specifically since we integrate over the unitary and orthogonal compact manifolds, facilitated via the Weyl integration formula and the Haar measure.

### [151] [EvalStop: Using World Feedback to Detect and Correct Reward Overoptimization in Multi-Tenant RLHF Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04145)
*Guilin Zhang,Chuanyi Sun,Shahryar Sarkani,John M. Fossaceca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 LLM RLHF 训练中普遍存在的“奖励过度优化”和计算资源浪费问题，研究提出了 EvalStop 调度原语。通过监控评估指标而非训练损失，它能精准识别并终止黑客行为，在显著减少计算浪费的同时提升了作业调度效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）训练中，模型存在“奖励过度优化”现象，即代理奖励模型与真实评估指标出现背离。现有平台调度器要么忽略这种质量偏差，要么使用不可靠的训练损失作为代理，导致严重的计算资源浪费。

Method: 提出了 EvalStop 调度原语，当评估分数连续 k 次下降时终止作业，释放 GPU 资源并保存最佳检查点。作者将其建模为检测问题，并在离散事件模拟器中进行了评估，重点关注在奖励黑客（reward-hacking）与正常训练任务混合负载下的表现。

Result: 在 RLHF 密集型工作负载下，EvalStop 实现了 98% 的精确率和 99% 的召回率，将 JCT 提高了 9%，并减少了 22% 的计算浪费。相比之下，传统的基于损失或固定进度的调度方法在处理正常任务时会产生极高的误报率，或无法捕获大部分黑客行为。

Conclusion: EvalStop 是一种有效的可组合调度原语，通过将“奖励过度优化”识别为检测问题，解决了 RLHF 工作负载中计算资源浪费的问题，在提高作业完成时间（JCT）的同时显著降低了资源损耗，是云端 LLM 微调平台中处理奖励黑客行为的理想方案。

Abstract: Cloud LLM fine-tuning platforms increasingly serve RLHF workloads, where a learned reward model is optimized as a proxy for human quality. As Gao et al. (2023) showed, this proxy diverges from world feedback (downstream eval metrics) under sustained optimization pressure, a phenomenon known as reward overoptimization. Existing platform schedulers ignore this divergence: non-clairvoyant schedulers optimize JCT without any quality signal, SLAQ-style quality-aware schedulers use training loss (a weaker proxy that drops monotonically through hacking), and classical per-job early stopping requires human monitoring and does not free shared GPUs. We propose EvalStop, a composable scheduling primitive that terminates jobs on k consecutive eval-score declines, releases GPUs, preserves the best checkpoint, and delegates to any base scheduler. We frame scheduler-level early stopping as a detection problem and evaluate it in a discrete-event simulator whose RLHF workload mixes reward-hacking and structurally healthy runs, with ground-truth labels hidden from schedulers. On RLHF-heavy workloads (80% RLHF, 64 GPUs), EvalStop achieves precision 98% / recall 99% / FPR 1.5% while improving JCT by 9% and cutting wasted compute by 22% over SRTF-Est (p<0.05). Trivial fixed-progress and loss-plateau competitors either incur 65% FPR on healthy RLHF or miss over half of true hacking cases. Gains compose across every base scheduler tested (9-25% JCT) and detection quality stays stable under eval noise (precision at least 91% at noise std <= 0.05) and hacking base rate (precision at least 89% across 20-80% hacking fractions).

</details>


### [152] [Physics-Informed Neural Network Modeling of Biodegradable Contaminant Transport through GCL/SL Composite Liners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04392)
*Dong Li,Yapeng Cao,Haiping Zhao,Shutong Han*

Two formulations are evaluated against analytical and finite-element reference solutions under different leachate-head conditions: a standard PINN with soft constraint enforcement (Std-PINN) and a hard-constrained PINN (H-PINN), in which selected boundary and initial conditions are embedded directly into the trial solutions. The Std-PINN captures the overall breakthrough behavior but shows larger errors during the early transport stage, particularly under higher leachate heads where advective transport becomes more pronounced. The H-PINN reduces the optimization burden associated with penalty-based constraint enforcement and provides more accurate and stable concentration predictions, lowering the MAE from approximately 0.058-0.067 for the Std-PINN to about 0.011-0.023 for the H-PINN, while reducing the MRE from approximately 9.10%-19.16% to about 2.08%-3.14%. Parametric analyses confirm that the H-PINN with the tanh activation function and an optimized network structure provides the best predictive accuracy. The H-PINN is further extended to inverse modeling for identifying the SL degradation half-life from limited concentration observations, showing reliable convergence toward prescribed values and acceptable robustness under low-to-moderate observation noise.

### [153] [DPDL: Towards Differential Privacy Preservation in Decentralized Stochastic Learning on Non-IID Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04399)
*Yunsheng Yuan,Xue Xiao,Lina Wang,Feng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对去中心化学习中的隐私泄露与数据 Non-IID 问题，提出了一种基于差分隐私与相似度校准的 DPDL 算法，在保护隐私的同时实现了高效的分布式模型训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在去中心化学习中，频繁的梯度交换导致严重的隐私泄露风险；同时，实际应用中数据通常呈现非独立同分布（Non-IID）特征，进一步增加了隐私保护与高效训练的难度。因此，需要一种能在 Non-IID 环境下有效保护隐私的去中心化学习方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DPDL 的算法。其核心是在每轮训练中，代理通过高斯噪声机制对跨梯度（即邻居模型在本地数据上的梯度）进行扰动，并利用余弦相似度对接收到的扰动跨梯度进行校准，最后以类似动量的方式更新本地模型，从而在隐私保护与模型性能之间取得平衡。

Result: 理论分析证明了该算法在实现特定隐私等级所需的最小噪声水平，并确认了其在 Non-IID 数据下仍能保持线性加速比。实验结果验证了 DPDL 在防御隐私攻击方面的有效性，以及在训练高精度模型方面的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 DPDL 算法通过在跨梯度聚合中引入差分隐私，并在非独立同分布（Non-IID）数据环境下结合相似度校准机制，有效地在保护代理隐私的同时，实现了高效且准确的去中心化模型训练，证明了在隐私约束下处理异构数据是可行的。

Abstract: In the paradigm of decentralized learning, a group of agents collaborate to train a global model using distributed datasets without a central server. Although the power of collaboration has been verified by many state-of-the-art studies, it entails extensive gradient information exchanging among the agents and thus induces high risk of privacy leakage for the individual agents. Moreover, in real-world applications, the training data are usually non-identically and independently distributed across the agents, inducing more challenges to enable privacy-preserved decentralized learning. To address these issues, we propose a privacy-preserved decentralized learning algorithm with non-IID data, DPDL, which leverages the notion of Differential Privacy (DP) in cross-gradient aggregation through a similarity-based calibration technique. Specifically, in each round, each agent perturbs the cross-gradients (i.e., the derivatives of its neighbors' local model in its private local data) by Gaussian noise mechanism before sharing them with its neighbors; it then adopt cosine similarity to calibrate the received perturbed cross-gradients such that the aggregation of the calibrated cross-gradients can be utilized to effectively update local model in a momentum-like manner. Our rigorous theoretical analysis not only reveals the minimum noise level required to achieve a specific level of privacy preservation, but also illustrates that our algorithm still achieves a linear speedup in training with non-IID data. We finally conduct extensive experiments on real-world dataset to validate the effectiveness of our algorithm in defending privacy attacks and in training accurate models.

</details>


### [154] [Smart Transportation Without Neurons -- Fair Metro Network Expansion with Tabular Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04167)
*Dimitris Michailidis,Sennay Ghebreab,Fernando P. Santos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对地铁网络扩展问题，本文提出了一种基于表格强化学习（Tabular RL）的非马尔可夫决策方法，在显著降低计算成本和碳排放的同时，实现了与深度强化学习相当的性能，并增强了模型的可解释性与公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的地铁网络扩展方法依赖专家定义的约束，搜索空间受限；而新兴的深度强化学习（Deep RL）虽能处理复杂序列决策，但存在计算成本高、环境负担重（高碳排放）以及模型黑箱（缺乏可解释性）等问题。研究者旨在通过研究证明，对于中小规模的MNEP，无需依赖复杂的深度学习，即可通过优化决策过程实现高性能与高效率。

Method: 1. 将地铁网络扩展问题（MNEP）重构为非马尔可夫奖励决策过程（NMRDP）。
2. 采用表格强化学习（Tabular RL）算法进行求解。
3. 在奖励函数中引入社会公平性指标（效率与公平），以平衡网络性能与社会效益。
4. 使用西安和阿姆斯特丹的真实交通数据进行模型评估与验证。

Result: 与深度强化学习（Deep RL）相比，该方法在保持相当性能的前提下，平均减少了18倍的训练轮次，并将碳排放降低了12倍，同时展现出了卓越的模型可解释性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了对于规模有限的地铁网络扩展问题（MNEP），使用基于表格的强化学习（Tabular RL）而非深度强化学习（Deep RL）是更优的选择。这种方法不仅显著提升了训练效率、降低了碳排放，还因其具备更高的可解释性和公平性考量，为解决组合优化问题提供了一种高效、可扩展且可持续的范式。

Abstract: We tackle the Metro Network Expansion Problem (MNEP), a subset of the Transport Network Design Problem (TNDP), which focuses on expanding metro systems to satisfy travel demand. Traditional methods rely on exact and heuristic approaches that require expert-defined constraints to reduce the search space. Recently, deep reinforcement learning (Deep RL) has emerged due to its effectiveness in complex sequential decision-making processes-it remains, however, computationally expensive, environmentally costly, and requires additional engineering to interpret. We show that MNEP problems are small enough to not require Deep RL methods. Reformulating the MNEP as a Non-Markovian Rewards Decision Process (NMRDP), we use tabular RL to achieve similar performance with significantly fewer training episodes, additionally offering greater interpretability. Additionally, we incorporate social equity criteria into the reward functions, focusing on efficiency and fairness, highlighting the versatility of our method. Evaluated in real-world settings-Xi'an and Amsterdam-our method reduces total episodes by a factor of 18 and total carbon emissions by a factor of 12 on average, while remaining competitive with Deep RL. This approach offers a replicable, modular, interpretable, and resource-efficient solution with potential applications to other combinatorial optimization problems.

### [155] [TANDEM: Bi-Level Data Mixture Optimization with Twin Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04401)
*Jiaxing Wang,Deping Xiang,Jin Xu,Mingyang Yi,Guoqiang Gong,Zicheng Zhang,Haoran Li,Pengzhang Liu,Zhen Chen,Ke Zhang,Ju Fan,Qixiang Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了TANDEM框架，通过双胞胎网络动态优化大语言模型的训练数据配比，有效提升了模型在多领域任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的性能高度依赖于训练数据的构成，如何优化多领域数据的混合比例是一个关键挑战，而现有的优化方法往往计算复杂且缺乏普适性。

Method: 提出了一种名为TANDEM的方法，将复杂的双层优化问题简化为单层惩罚形式，利用双胞胎网络（代理模型与参考模型）进行训练，并通过两者之间的差异评估数据的有效性，从而动态优化领域数据混合比例。

Result: 实验证明，TANDEM在多种场景（如数据受限、监督微调等）下均能有效优化数据混合比例，并显著提升大语言模型的性能，同时具备理论保证和更广泛的适用性。

Conclusion: TANDEM通过双层优化视角解决了大模型训练中的数据配比问题，证明了动态调整领域权重能显著提升模型性能，并为后续研究数据分配策略提供了新的理论与应用框架。

Abstract: The capabilities of large language models (LLMs) significantly depend on training data drawn from various domains. Optimizing domain-specific mixture ratios can be modeled as a bi-level optimization problem, which we simplify into a single-level penalized form and solve with twin networks: a proxy model trained on primary data and a dynamically updated reference model trained with additional data. Our proposed method, Twin Networks for bi-level DatA mixturE optiMization (TANDEM), measures the data efficacy through the difference between the twin models and up-weights domains that benefit more from the additional data. TANDEM provides theoretical guarantees and wider applicability, compared to prior approaches. Furthermore, our bi-level perspective suggests new settings to study domain reweighting such as data-restricted scenarios and supervised fine-tuning, where optimized mixture ratios significantly improve the performance. Extensive experiments validate TANDEM's effectiveness in all scenarios.

### [156] [Low-Rank Decay for Grokking in Scale-Invariant Transformers: A Spectral-Geometric View](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04405)
*Mingyu Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对Transformer架构中归一化导致L2权重衰减失效的问题，提出了一种新型的“低秩衰减”（LRD）方法，通过利用核范数特性在权重空间产生切向优化，有效促进了模型的结构压缩与泛化表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代Transformer架构中，由于采用了RMSNorm等归一化机制，模型权重具备标度不变性，导致传统的Frobenius范数（L2）权重衰减在训练后期失效，无法有效简化函数表示，也无法通过改变权重谱来促进泛化。因此需要一种新的正则化手段来突破这一限制。

Method: 本文提出了“低秩衰减”（Low-Rank Decay, LRD）算法，这是一种类似于核范数的谱正则化方法。其核心机制在于通过计算权重矩阵的极分解（Polar factor $UV^\top$）来施加惩罚，从而在模型具备标度不变性的情况下，仍能在权重空间中产生切向分量，持续压缩奇异值。

Result: 在模运算任务中，LRD成功诱导了Query/Key矩阵的有效秩快速收敛（rank collapse），显著扩大了模型发生延迟泛化（grokking）的数据规模边界，并从谱几何角度阐释了核范数次微分在低秩层附近的“针到扇”（needle-to-fan）扩展机制。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过采用针对标度不变性优化的低秩正则化（LRD），可以有效克服传统L2权重衰减在归一化架构中的局限性。LRD不仅在训练后期具备持续优化权矩阵谱的能力，还能通过促进奇异值压缩显著提升模型的泛化能力和“顿悟”（grokking）现象的表现。

Abstract: Modern Transformer architectures frequently employ normalization mechanisms such as RMSNorm and Query-Key Normalization, making parts of the model approximately scale-invariant with respect to weight magnitudes. In this regime, standard Frobenius-norm weight decay acts purely along the radial direction of the weight space and cannot directly simplify the function represented by the normalized layer. We study grokking in small algorithmic tasks through this lens and propose \emph{Low-Rank Decay} (LRD), a nuclear-norm-like spectral regularizer whose subgradient -- the polar factor $UV^\top$ -- retains a tangential component even in the scale-invariant setting. This distinction has a concrete dynamical consequence: after the model memorizes the training set and task gradients vanish, L2 decay can no longer reshape the weight spectrum, whereas LRD continues to compress singular values in an $\ell_1$-like fashion. On modular arithmetic tasks, we find that LRD induces rapid effective-rank collapse in Query/Key matrices and expands the data-fraction boundary at which delayed generalization (grokking) occurs. We further provide a spectral-geometric interpretation through the ``needle-to-fan'' expansion of the nuclear-norm subdifferential near low-rank strata.

</details>


### [157] [An Ensembled Latent Factor Model via Differential Evolution and Gradient Descent Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04408)
*Rui Zhang,Jinhang Liu,Wenbo Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维不完整（HDI）数据在现实应用中广泛存在。现有潜因子模型多单一依赖梯度下降进行优化，容易导致在高维异构数据场景下产生表征不足或产生偏差的问题。因此，需要引入新的优化范式来改善潜因子表征的质量。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ELFM-DEGDO 的集成潜因子模型。该方法由两个核心步骤组成：首先，分别利用差分进化算法和梯度下降法独立构建两个不同的潜因子模型；其次，设计了一种定制化的自适应加权机制，将上述两个模型进行融合，以结合不同优化策略的互补优势。

Result: 通过在三个 HDI 数据集上的实验测试，结果表明 ELFM-DEGDO 在表征学习任务中表现出比现有主流潜因子模型更优越且一致的性能。

Conclusion: ELFM-DEGDO 成功整合了差异进化和梯度下降两种优化范式的优势，为高维不完整数据提供了更全面、偏差更小的表征学习方法，显著提升了模型性能。

Abstract: High-dimensional and incomplete (HDI) data are prevalent in many real-world big data scenarios. Latent factor models serve as a common representation learning approach, capable of uncovering informative latent factors from such data. Nevertheless, most existing latent factor models rely solely on gradient descent for optimization, which may lead to insufficient and biased representations, particularly when dealing with heterogeneous HDI data. Thus, this study proposes an Ensembled Latent Factor Model via Differential Evolution and Gradient Descent Optimization (ELFM-DEGDO) with two-fold designed: 1) two diverse latent factor models are independently modeled via differential evolution and gradient descent optimization, respectively, and 2) the two diverse latent factor models are combined via a customized self-adaptive weighting mechanism to effectively fuse their strengths. By leveraging the complementary advantages of both optimization paradigms, ELFM-DEGDO is able to produce more comprehensive and less biased representations for HDI data. Three HDI datasets are tested to show that ELFM-DEGDO consistently performs better than related several latent factor models.

### [158] [Dual Advantage Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04188)
*Alexey Zemtsov,Maxim Bobrin,Alexander Nikulin,Dmitry V. Dylov,Fakhri Karray,Vladislav Kurenkov,Martin Takáč,Arip Asadulaev*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对离线目标条件RL，本文提出了双优势场（DAF）方法，通过将双线性对偶值模型转化为局部优势信号，在保持全局可达性评估的同时，实现了更精确的局部动作决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离线目标条件强化学习方法通常使用双目标表示来捕获全局目标可达性，但这些方法无法直接指明在给定状态下应采取何种最优局部动作，导致在需要精细动作规划的任务中表现受限。

Method: 提出“双优势场”（Dual Advantage Fields, DAF）。通过学习一个动作-效果模型（action-effect model）来预测动作带来的折扣特征位移，并将该位移与目标方向进行对齐得分，从而将双线性对偶值模型转化为局部优势函数，实现策略提取。

Result: 在OGBench的运动、操作和拼图任务中，DAF在RLiable指标上取得了显著提升，特别是在局部最优动作与最终目标方向不一致的复杂场景下表现卓越。

Conclusion: DAF通过将双线性对偶值模型转化为局部优势信号，有效地解决了离线目标条件强化学习中全局可达性估计与局部动作选择之间的脱节问题，在多种任务中展现了优于传统方法的性能。

Abstract: Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning requires both long-horizon reachability estimates and local action comparisons. Dual goal representations provide value fields that capture global goal reachability, but they do not directly specify which action should be preferred at a given state. We propose Dual Advantage Fields, a policy-extraction method that turns a bilinear dual value model into a local advantage signal. Under bilinear dual parameterization, the goal embedding is the gradient of the value field with respect to the state representation. DAF learns an action-effect model that predicts the discounted feature displacement induced by an action and scores actions by the alignment between this displacement and the goal direction. In the realizable case, this score equals the goal-conditioned Bellman advantage, yielding a standard local policy-improvement guarantee. On OGBench locomotion, manipulation, and puzzle tasks, DAF improves aggregate RLiable metrics and performs strongly in settings where locally correct actions differ from direct movement toward the final goal.

</details>


### [159] [(Mis)generalization of Helpful-only Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04413)
*Mohammad Omar Khursheed,Baram Sosis,Fabien Roger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入分析了“仅提供帮助”模型在对齐方面的短板，指出直接的抗拒绝训练会导致模型出现谄媚和角色混乱等问题，并证明了通过改进微调方法和训练数据策略，可以在保持高帮助性的同时优化模型的整体表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: “仅提供帮助”模型在人工智能研发和危险能力评估中具有重要应用价值，但目前对于此类模型在除了“拒绝行为”以外的其他对齐维度（如可控性、诚实度等）上的泛化能力和潜在缺陷缺乏深入了解。

Method: 研究人员通过评估现有“仅提供帮助”模型在失调、剩余拒绝行为、可控性、谄媚倾向及角色一致性等维度的表现，揭示了简单的抗拒绝训练（anti-refusal training）带来的负面效应，并提出通过合成文档微调（synthetic document fine-tuning）及优化SFT与RL的数据集设计来改进模型。

Result: 研究发现，现有的“仅提供帮助”模型普遍存在紧急失调（emergent misalignment）、残留拒绝行为、可控性差、谄媚（sycophancy）以及角色不连贯等问题。此外，简单的抗拒绝训练往往是导致这些问题的根源。

Conclusion: “仅提供帮助”（Helpful-only）模型并不必然导致失调。通过采用合成文档微调以及在有监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）阶段加入与角色相关的问答，可以有效缓解模型出现的偏见、谄媚及不一致性等缺陷，从而构建出既具备高帮助性又表现良好的模型。

Abstract: Helpful-only models, that is, models that are trained to always follow user intent, are valuable for dangerous capability evaluations and other areas of AI R&D where refusals would be an obstacle. Little is known about the generalization properties of helpful-only training: helpful-only models refuse less than their harmless counterparts, but previous work has not studied other dimensions of their alignment. We study the shortcomings of existing helpful-only models. We find that some show emergent misalignment, others have residual refusal behaviors, and most show poor steerability, sycophancy, and incoherent character. We show that simple anti-refusal training can cause many of these issues. None of these problems are necessary consequences of helpful-only training, though: we show that synthetic document fine-tuning and adding character-related questions to SFT and RL can mitigate them.
