<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer在处理多通道标量信号时，需要将C个同时发生的值嵌入到d_model维度的向量中。目前尚缺乏对不同多通道输入编码方案的系统性评估，研究旨在揭示哪种编码方式在性能和效率上表现最优。

Method: 研究人员构建了一个包含八种不同输入编码器（包括线性投影、MLP主干、通道独立等架构）的评估框架，并在合成数据集（设计用于测试通道标识的重要性）和ETTh1真实数据集上进行基准测试，通过比较下个时间步的负对数似然（NLL）来衡量性能。

Result: 实验表明，大多数“顶级”编码器性能差异微小，标准的逐通道线性投影表现均衡且稳健。共享标量基线因信息丢失而表现极差，通道独立架构（PatchTST风格）在两个基准测试中均表现不佳并存在过拟合问题。在特定情况下，带有学习线性层的正弦位置编码或非线性MLP主干会有微弱优势，但总体而言，简单线性投影已足够应对大多数场景。

Conclusion: 在处理多通道标量信号时，标准的逐通道线性投影（nn.Linear(C, d_model)）是性价比最高、最稳健的选择。除非任务有特殊需求，否则无需使用更复杂的编码方案。共享标量基线和通道独立架构在性能上明显劣于该标准方法。

Abstract: Transformers consuming multi-channel scalar signals must embed $C$ simultaneous values into one $d_{\text{model}}$-dimensional vector per time step. We empirically audit eight input encoders -- spanning a shared-scalar baseline, per-channel linear projections, an orthogonality regulariser, a nonlinear MLP stem, block-partitioned concatenation, channel-independent and channel-as-token architectures, and a projected positional encoding -- on a synthetic benchmark designed to make channel identity informative and on ETTh1 as a real-data check, measured in next-step negative log-likelihood (NLL). The headline is one of practical near-equivalence within a wide "top tier": the standard per-channel linear projection (nn.Linear(C, $d_{\text{model}}$)) matches every alternative in that tier up to small, statistically real but practically modest, differences. Two encoders lose decisively: the shared-scalar baseline, which collapses for information-theoretic reasons we make explicit, and the channel-independent PatchTST-spirit baseline, which underperforms on both benchmarks and overfits universally on the synthetic one. Paired tests resolve two small gaps: projecting the sinusoidal positional encoding through a learned linear layer edges the rest at small $C$, with a direct geometric probe showing the mechanism is positional-channel orthogonalisation; a nonlinear MLP stem edges them at the largest $C$ we test, with the gap shrinking under more training data. The practical recommendation is to use nn.Linear(C, $d_{\text{model}}$) by default and reach for something more elaborate only when the task at hand gives a real reason to do so. Code and data to reproduce every experiment in this paper are available at https://github.com/OssiLehtinen/channel-encoder-audit

</details>


### [200] [Validity Threats for Foundation Model Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05029)
*Gunnar König,Martin Pawelczyk,Ulrike von Luxburg,Sebastian Bordt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对大型基础模型训练昂贵的问题，评估了各种低成本研究替代方案（如代理实验、观察性研究等）所带来的效度威胁，并提出了一个基于因果推断框架的工具包，旨在帮助研究人员系统地识别和应对这些方法论上的隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基础模型规模的扩大，传统的受控实验变得极其昂贵，研究社区转而采用代理实验、观察性研究等低成本替代策略。然而，这些策略往往伴随着难以察觉或未经检验的假设，可能导致研究结论失效，因此迫切需要一套评估这些替代方案有效性的框架。

Method: 本文提出一个评估框架，将基础模型研究视作因果推断问题，并从社会科学领域引入四类效度标准（统计效度、内部效度、外部效度、构念效度）来系统地审查代理实验、观察性研究及单次运行设计等研究策略的有效性。

Result: 研究发现每种替代策略都有其固有的“效度配置”：代理实验以牺牲外部和构念效度为代价换取统计和内部效度；观察性研究受到混淆变量和效应异质性的影响；单次运行设计则受限于处理单元间的干扰。该分析揭示了目前文献中被忽视的多个关键效度威胁。

Conclusion: 在基础模型研究中，“免费午餐”是不存在的。每种节省计算资源的替代性实验策略都伴随着特定的效度威胁。通过将模型研究视为因果推断问题，研究者可以更系统地评估并规避这些风险，从而提升研究设计的严谨性。

Abstract: Controlled experiments are the backbone of machine learning research, but at the scale of modern foundation models, they have become prohibitively expensive. Instead, the community increasingly relies on research strategies that approximate the ideal experiment at a fraction of the cost: proxy experiments and scaling laws, observational studies with publicly available models, and single-run designs that leverage variation within individual training runs. In this work, we argue that there is no free lunch when approximating large-scale experiments on a compute budget. Specifically, savings in compute come at the cost of validity threats -- hidden and sometimes untestable assumptions that, when violated, can invalidate research claims. To help navigate such threats, we propose an evaluation framework that casts foundation model research as a causal inference problem. Within this framework, we evaluate different research strategies through four types of validity adapted from the empirical social sciences -- statistical, internal, external, and construct validity. We find that each strategy comes with a characteristic validity profile: proxy experiments trade external and construct validity for statistical and internal validity; observational studies face confounding and effect heterogeneity; and single-run designs are strained by interference between treated units. This analysis reveals several validity threats that have received insufficient attention in the literature. Overall, our evaluation framework provides researchers with a practical toolkit for scrutinizing validity threats in foundation model research~designs.

</details>


### [201] [Beyond Structural Symmetries: Linear Mode Connectivity via Neuron Identifiability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04754)
*Vincent Bürgin,Daniel Herbst,Ya-Wei Eileen Lin,Stefanie Jegelka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“有效函数类”框架，定量分析了神经元对称性对损失函数景观及训练动力学的影响，解释了神经网络在不同训练路径下如何通过神经元可识别性实现表征合并与线性模式连接。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管深度学习中存在线性模式连接性等现象，但参数对称性与具体数据、模型表征之间的确切机制尚不明确。研究者旨在填补这一空白，探索神经元层面的对称性如何影响训练动态和损失函数景观。

Method: 1. 构建了“有效函数类”理论框架，通过神经元在其输入支持上能实现的函数集合及其实现的范数代价来量化表征；2. 定义了“有效对称性破缺”（effective symmetry breaking）概念，用于衡量不同训练过程中神经元的可识别性；3. 利用这些工具分析了参数空间、数据分布与模型表征之间的相互作用。

Result: 1. 证明了即使在结构上不对称的模型中，神经网络也存在大量近似等价的解；2. 表明神经元的可识别性使得无需预对齐即可进行表征合并（representation merging）；3. 阐明了特定条件下，这种表征合并能够产生通往低损失区域的线性路径。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了参数对称性与“有效函数类”之间的深层联系，证明了神经元的可识别性（identifiability）是理解模型损失函数空间结构（如线性连接性）的关键，为解析深度学习训练动力学提供了一个统一的理论视角。

Abstract: Many striking phenomena in deep learning, such as linear mode connectivity and the structured behavior of training dynamics, are closely tied to parameter symmetries: transformations that leave the realized function unchanged. Despite growing attention to parameter symmetries, the exact interplay between parameters, data, and representations remains underexplored. To investigate this, we develop a theoretical framework of effective function classes, i.e., the set of functions a neuron can realize on its input support, and the norm cost of realizing them. We then formalize effective symmetry breaking via neuron identifiability across independent training runs. Our analysis shows that neural networks can admit large families of approximately equivalent solutions even in structurally asymmetric models. We further show that neuron identifiability enables representation merging without prior alignment, and characterize when such merging admits a linear low-loss path. These findings highlight the role of effective function classes in affecting the loss landscape.

### [202] [In-Context Graphical Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05042)
*Zehua Cheng,Wei Dai,Jiahao Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对离散图模型推断在高树宽和挫折拓扑下存在的精确性与收敛性矛盾，该论文提出了 ICG-I 模型，通过模拟变量消元法的自回归 Graph Transformer 结构，实现了高精度推断并提供了统计校准保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离散图模型推断中，现有方法存在“精确性”与“可扩展性”的两难困境：精确算法在高树宽图形上计算不可行，而迭代近似算法（如置信传播 BP）在处理具有挫折（frustrated）拓扑结构的图形时往往难以保证收敛，作者认为这是由于迭代方法放弃了精确推断所需的顺序消元结构。

Method: 提出了一种名为“上下文内图形推断”（In-Context Graphical Inference, ICG-I）的自回归 Graph Transformer。其核心在于：1. 模仿变量消元法（Variable Elimination）的顺序执行过程；2. 利用张量列（Tensor-Train）压缩技术处理中间因子；3. 引入狄利克雷输出层；4. 结合加权共形预测（Weighted Conformal Prediction）以提供分布偏移下的校准保证。

Result: ICG-I 在所有基准测试中均达到了 SOTA 水平。在标准实例上将平均绝对误差（MAE）从 0.041 降低至 0.020；在 BP 完全发散的 N=500 挫折自旋玻璃模型上，取得了 0.048 的优异表现。理论上证明了 TT 压缩误差的线性传播性，并证明了模型在特定条件下的覆盖保证。

Conclusion: ICG-I 成功地将变量消元法的结构与 Transformer 的表征能力相结合，为高树宽和具有挫折拓扑结构的图模型推断提供了一种高效、精确且具有校准保证的新范式，并在多种基准测试中超越了传统算法。

Abstract: Marginal inference in discrete graphical models forces a choice between exactness and scalability: exact algorithms are intractable for high-treewidth graphs, while iterative approximations (Belief Propagation, variational methods) sacrifice convergence guarantees on frustrated topologies. We argue that this dichotomy stems from a mismatched inductive bias: iterative methods abandon the sequential elimination structure that makes exact inference correct. We introduce In-Context Graphical Inference (ICG-I), an autoregressive Graph Transformer that restores this structure by mimicking Variable Elimination with learned, Tensor- Train-compressed intermediate factors, paired with a Dirichlet output layer and Weighted Conformal Prediction for calibrated, distribution-free coverage guarantees under topological shift. We prove that TT compression errors propagate at most lincarly through the autoregressive chain, that the Dirichlet-Multinomial loss is a proper scoring rule, and that WCP maintains coverage with a quantifiable degradation under estimated density ratios. We conducted intensive experiments to evaluate ICG-I and achieved state-of-the-art performance across all benchmarks. ICG-I reduces MAE from 0.041 (best baseline) to 0.020 on standard instances and achieves 0.048 on N=500 frustrated spin glasses where BP diverges entirely.

</details>


### [203] [Measuring Model Robustness via Fisher Information: Spectral Bounds, Theoretical Guarantees, and Practical Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04767)
*Chong Zhang,Xiang Li,Jia Wang,Qiufeng Wang,Xiaobo Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于费舍尔信息矩阵（FIM）谱范数的攻击无关型鲁棒性度量方法，通过量化模型输出分布对输入扰动的最差情况敏感度，为深度学习模型提供了一种高效、可解释的鲁棒性评估与诊断方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度神经网络鲁棒性评估方法高度依赖于特定的对抗攻击手段，缺乏可解释性，难以全面评估模型在不受控环境下的表现。因此，作者旨在提出一种与攻击无关、具有理论支撑且具备可解释性的鲁棒性评估指标。

Method: 1. 理论推导：证明了FIM等价于输入雅可比矩阵的方差，并为VGG、ResNet、DenseNet和Transformer等常见架构推导出闭式谱界。
2. 算法设计：提出了基于幂迭代（Power Iteration）和Hutchinson估计的高效算法，支持白盒与黑盒评估设置。
3. 实验验证：在CIFAR、ImageNet及医疗影像数据集上，将该指标与实际对抗脆弱性进行了相关性分析。

Result: 1. 建立了首个基于模型架构的理论鲁棒性排名。
2. 实验结果表明，所提出的基于FIM谱范数的指标与模型的对抗脆弱性之间具有高度相关性。
3. 提供了高效的工具，能够在不同规模的模型（如ImageNet级别的架构）上实现鲁棒性评估。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于费舍尔信息矩阵（FIM）谱范数的鲁棒性评估框架，克服了传统对抗攻击评估的局限性。该方法不仅在理论上为不同架构提供了鲁棒性排名，还通过高效的算法在实际应用中验证了其有效性，为深度学习模型的鲁棒性设计与诊断提供了一个可解释且通用的评估工具。

Abstract: The robustness of deep neural networks is crucial for safety-critical deployments, yet existing evaluation methods are often attack-dependent and lack interpretability. We propose a principled, attack-agnostic robustness metric based on the spectral norm of the Fisher Information Matrix (FIM), which quantifies the worst-case sensitivity of the model's output distribution to input perturbations. Theoretically, we establish that the FIM equals the variance of the input Jacobian and derive closed-form spectral bounds for common architectures, including VGG, ResNet, DenseNet, and Transformer, providing the first theoretical robustness ranking. To enable scalable evaluation, we develop efficient algorithms, including power iteration and Hutchinson-based estimation, that support both white-box and black-box settings. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets, including CIFAR, ImageNet, and medical images, and across multiple architectures show a strong correlation between our metric and adversarial vulnerability. Our framework serves as an interpretable diagnostic tool that complements attack-based evaluations, offering insights into architectural sensitivity and guiding the design of more robust models. Code is available at: https://github.com/franz-chang/SRP/.

### [204] [Failed Reasoning Traces Tell You What Is Fixable (But Not by Reading Them)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05145)
*Nizar Islah,Istabrak Abbes,Irina Rish,Sarath Chandar,Eilif B. Muller*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过分析模型失败轨迹分布来诊断推理错误的方法，能有效区分随机错误与结构性错误，并通过无需训练的路由策略显著提升了模型在复杂推理任务中的补救效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时扩展（test-time scaling）策略在模型推理失败时，往往仅通过增加重采样次数（rollouts）来试图解决问题，忽略了失败轨迹本身蕴含的诊断信息。许多失败属于结构性缺陷，单纯增加计算量无法解决。因此，作者旨在从失败轨迹中识别出其“可恢复性结构”，以便针对性地选择合适的补救干预手段。

Method: 作者基于失败采样轨迹的分布特征（而非文本内容），提取了三个问题层面的轨迹特征。利用这些特征对模型失败进行聚类，区分出“可通过重采样解决”和“需要结构性干预”的失败类型。随后，基于此开发了一套无需额外训练的路由规则，在测试时自动为失败案例选择最优的补救方案。

Result: 该方法能够以 84.3% 的准确率对失败类型进行分类（较基线提升 20%）。在 Steerable-Hard 子集上，其路由规则使模型补救成功率提升了 12.2%。此外，该方法在跨模型家族的实验中表现出良好的迁移性，无需获取模型权重或进行额外的训练。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一套无需训练的诊断与路由框架，通过分析失败推理路径的分布特征来区分“运气不佳”与“结构性失败”，从而实现了更有效的测试时干预。这证明了模型失败轨迹本身蕴含着重要的诊断价值，为提升大模型推理可靠性提供了新范式。

Abstract: When post-trained language models fail on reasoning problems, the common test-time-scaling response is to spend more compute on additional attempts, and the failed traces play no further role. We argue this discards a crucial signal; some failures come from unlucky sampling, where more rollouts help, while others are structural and resist resampling regardless of budget. We propose that failed traces encode recoverability structure: the inference-time signature of which test-time interventions can rescue a given failure. Three problem-level trajectory features, derived from the structure of available interventions, recover this structure from the distributional signature of failed rollouts, not their text. They cluster failures into stable regimes, characterize the failure topography of different post-training methods ($84.3{\pm}4.3\%$ accuracy, $+20\%$ over a majority-class baseline), and support a training-free routing rule that lifts rescue by $+12.2\%$ on the deployment-relevant Steerable-Hard subset (failures where retry is insufficient and a bounded intervention is reachable). The features and the routing rule transfer across two cross-family probes. The same three features thus convert failed traces from discarded data into a diagnostic object, supporting test-time routing and post-training analysis without training-time or weight-space access.

### [205] [Activation Steering of Video Generation Models via Reduced-Order Linear Optimal Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04775)
*Jihoon Hong,Alice Chan,Qiyue Dai,Julian Skifstad,Glen Chou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有文本生成视频模型干预手段粗糙、易导致质量下降的问题，本文提出了一种基于隐空间线性二次调节器（LA-LQR）的微创控制框架，通过在低维子空间进行精确的最优控制，在提升生成内容安全性的同时保持了原始画质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本生成视频（T2V）模型的激活转向方法通常较为粗糙且缺乏预见性，容易导致模型输出过度转向或视频质量下降。为此，研究者希望通过最优控制理论，在不牺牲视觉质量的前提下，实现对模型生成内容的精准、微创干预，从而降低有害内容的产生。

Method: 提出了一种基于“隐空间线性二次调节器”（LA-LQR）的降阶最优控制框架。该方法首先将视频生成的激活值投影到由对比提示对导出的低维子空间中，然后在该隐空间内估计局部线性动力学，并求解线性二次调节器问题，从而计算出随时间步和层级变化的反馈控制信号，以实现最小化干扰下的精准转向。

Result: 在概念转向和视频安全性基准测试中，LA-LQR 相比现有基准方法显著降低了不安全内容的生成率，同时保持了良好的提示词忠实度和视频视觉质量。理论证明也证实了该方法在隐空间跟踪与原始激活空间特征控制之间的相关性。

Conclusion: LA-LQR 提供了一种高效、微创的视频生成模型控制框架，通过最优控制理论解决了传统激活转向方法中的过度控制和画质衰减问题，为提升文本生成视频模型的安全性和可控性提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Text-to-video (T2V) models trained on large-scale web data can generate undesired content, motivating interventions that reduce harmful outputs without sacrificing visual quality. Activation steering offers an attractive mechanistic alternative to finetuning and prompt filtering, but existing T2V steering methods remain limited, typically applying coarse, non-anticipative interventions that can lead to oversteering and content degradation. To close this gap, we propose Latent Activation Linear-Quadratic Regulator (LA-LQR), a reduced-order optimal control framework for minimally invasive T2V steering. LA-LQR formulates T2V inference as a dynamical system and computes closed-loop feedback interventions that steer activations toward desired feature setpoints while penalizing unnecessary perturbations. To make optimal control feasible for high-dimensional video activations, we project activations onto a low-dimensional, task-relevant subspace derived from contrastive prompt pairs, estimate local linear dynamics in this latent space, and solve a latent LQR problem to obtain timestep- and layer-specific steering signals. We provide theoretical bounds relating latent setpoint tracking to raw activation-space feature control, and empirically validate the fidelity of the reduced latent dynamics. On concept steering and video safety benchmarks, LA-LQR reduces unsafe generations relative to baselines, while preserving prompt fidelity and visual quality.

### [206] [Reinforcement Learning from Rich Feedback with Distributional DAgger](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05152)
*Rishabh Agrawal,Jacob Fein-Ashley,Paria Rashidinejad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对现有的推理模型训练方法（RLVR）奖励反馈稀疏且缺乏单调提升保障的问题，提出了一种名为DistIL的分布式模仿学习方法。该方法通过前向交叉熵目标函数有效利用多维专家反馈，实现了更好的信用分配，并保证了策略的单调提升，在多个推理任务中取得了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的推理模型训练主要依赖于仅基于最终结果正确与否的强化学习（RLVR），这种方法奖励信号稀疏且无法利用丰富的中间反馈信息（如工具使用痕迹、修正意见等）。此外，现有的基于逆向KL散度或Jensen-Shannon散度的自蒸馏RL方法在策略提升上缺乏理论上的单调性保证。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于DAgger算法的分布变体方法，称为DistIL。其核心在于利用专家轨迹（如执行记录、工具输出等）作为反馈，通过前向交叉熵目标函数实现策略优化，并利用序列级梯度进行更细致的信用分配（credit assignment），直接对学生模型和专家模型在状态上的不一致进行学习。

Result: 实验结果表明，DistIL在科学推理、代码生成及数学问题解决等任务中，显著优于传统的RLVR方法以及基于自蒸馏的强化学习基线模型，提升了模型的Pass@N指标。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DistIL方法通过使用前向交叉熵目标函数，不仅克服了传统RLVR中奖励信号稀疏的局限，还解决了自蒸馏目标函数无法保证策略单调提升的问题。DistIL不仅在理论上提供了遗憾度（regret）界，在科学推理、编程和数学问题等多个领域也表现出了比现有RLVR和自蒸馏方法更优的性能。

Abstract: Reasoning models have advanced rapidly, but the dominant reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) recipe remains surprisingly narrow: sample many responses and reward each with a single bit indicating whether the final answer is correct. Yet many settings provide rich feedback, including execution traces, tool outputs, expert corrections, and model self-evaluations. We study how to use such feedback through a distributional variant of the classic imitation learning algorithm DAgger, where the learner has local access to an expert distribution on states visited by the current policy. This yields a simple forward cross-entropy objective that admits a blackbox expert and whose sequence-level gradient {conduct rich credit assignment by propagating} future expert-student disagreement back to earlier decisions. We show that prior RL with self-distillation objectives based on reverse KL or Jensen-Shannon fail to guarantee monotonic policy improvement: even when the expert has higher reward, their updates may increase probability on worse actions. In contrast, we show that forward cross-entropy admits monotonic policy improvement and enjoys guarantees on regret. We further show that our objective optimizes a lower bound on teacher-weighted likelihood of success, leading to improved Pass@N. Empirically, our approach, DistIL, improves over RLVR and RL with self-distillation baselines across a variety of domains: scientific reasoning, coding, and solving hard mathematical problems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出名为 UniFair 的统一框架，联合优化分离公平性（增加受保护群体与决策边界的距离）和社会公平性（缩小群体间聚类代价的差异）；利用基于梯度的优化方法，并将其扩展至自动编码器的潜在空间进行深度聚类。

Conclusion: UniFair 提供了一个灵活且统一的框架，能够平衡聚类损失与不同维度的公平性（分离公平性和社会公平性），证明了在不牺牲太多聚类性能的前提下，通过梯度优化手段有效缓解群体不平等是可行的。

Abstract: Clustering is increasingly used to support high-impact decisions, yet standard objectives such as $k$-means can produce clusterings that treat demographic groups unequally. Existing fair clustering methods typically optimize a single notion of fairness and often overlook how clustering costs interact with the geometry of the induced decision boundaries. We propose \textsc{UniFair}, a unified framework that jointly optimizes \emph{separation fairness} and \emph{social fairness}. Separation fairness encourages protected groups to lie farther from the induced decision boundaries, while social fairness reduces disparities in within-cluster distortion by penalizing group-wise clustering costs. We develop gradient-based optimization procedures for separation-fair and unified $k$-means objectives, and extend them to deep clustering by enforcing the same criteria in the latent space of an autoencoder. Experiments on tabular and image datasets show that \textsc{UniFair} reduces both boundary-related and cost-based group disparities with only a modest increase in clustering loss.

### [208] [STRIDE: Training Data Attribution via Sparse Recovery from Subset Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05165)
*Rishit Dagli,Abir Harrasse,Luke Zhang,Florent Draye,Amirali Abdullah,Bernhard Schölkopf,Zhijing Jin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型（LLM）的训练数据归因方法存在主要痛点：基于因果干预的重训练法计算成本过高，而基于梯度近似的方法在大规模参数空间下计算压力极大且精度有限，因此需要一种更高效且具备局部影响捕捉能力的替代方案。

Method: 本文提出了STRIDE框架，将训练数据归因（TDA）建模为压缩感知中的稀疏恢复问题。该方法避开了在参数空间进行昂贵的梯度计算，转而在激活空间学习轻量级的“转向算子”（steering operators），这些算子用于模拟特定数据子集对模型行为的影响，并通过稀疏线性分解恢复单个训练样本的贡献度。

Result: STRIDE在大语言模型预训练归因任务中达到了最先进的性能（SOTA），其执行速度比现有技术快13倍，并成功应用于数据筛选、数据污染检测及定性分析等实际场景。

Abstract: Training Data Attribution (TDA) seeks to trace a model's predictions back to its training data. The gold standard for TDA relies on causal interventions, observing how a model changes when data is added or removed, but repeated retraining is computationally challenging for Large Language Models (LLMs). Consequently, most approaches approximate this effect in the parameter space using gradients. However, tracking gradients across billions of parameters is not only prohibitively expensive but relies on local approximations. In this work, we propose a shift: rather than estimating parameter changes, we model the functional effect of training data in the activation space. We introduce STRIDE (Steering-based Training Data Influence Decomposition), a framework that formulates TDA as a sparse recovery problem in the spirit of compressive sensing. STRIDE learns lightweight "steering operators" that mimic the behavioral shift caused by training on data subsets. By measuring how these operators perturb test predictions, we recover individual training example influences via sparse linear decomposition. STRIDE achieves state-of-the-art for LLM pre-training attribution while being an order of magnitude ($13\times$) faster than previous art. We further validate its practical utility through downstream applications including data selection, data contamination, and qualitative analysis.

### [210] [The Right Measure for Physics-Constrained Generation: A Co-Area Correction for Posterior-Consistent PDE Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04804)
*Jian Xu,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，目前在PDE反问题中强行应用硬物理约束来引导生成模型的做法在数学上是错误的，因为它忽略了必须的Fixman雅可比修正因子。作者提出了CoCoS算法，通过考虑测度一致性，成功纠正了这一偏差，实现了准确的后验不确定性采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式模型（如扩散模型和流匹配）被广泛用于求解偏微分方程（PDE）反问题，通常将物理定律作为“硬约束”强加给模型。然而，这种处理方式在统计学上存在严重偏差（Borel-Kolmogorov悖论），且忽略了正确的物理后验分布所需的雅可比因子，导致生成的后验结果在量化不确定性时存在显著的物理性偏差。作者旨在指出这一普遍存在的错误，并提供修正方案。

Method: 本文采用了理论分析与数值验证相结合的方法。首先，利用Borel-Kolmogorov悖论分析了在测度为零的流形上进行条件化的数学模糊性；其次，推导出了物理约束采样过程中必须包含的共面积（Fixman）雅可比因子 $[det(JJ^{\top})]^{-1/2}$；最后，开发了名为CoCoS的测度感知约束采样算法，并通过与i.i.d.基准结果的对照实验，验证了该方法在纠正采样偏差方面的有效性。

Result: 研究结果表明，现有的硬约束采样方法存在重大偏差：投影法和引导法产生的后验误差分别达到了采样噪声基准的20倍和9倍，且简单的标量重加权无法解决该问题。相比之下，作者提出的CoCoS方法能够准确逼近真实的后验分布，其采样误差仅在采样噪声水平之内，验证了理论推导的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了当前基于扩散模型和流匹配的物理约束PDE反问题求解方法在数学上的缺陷。作者指出，简单地将物理方程作为硬约束进行投影或引导，会忽略必要的测度校正因子（Fixman Jacobian），导致采样结果偏离真实的贝叶斯后验分布。提出的CoCoS算法通过显式包含该修正项，能够实现正确的后验采样，证明了“满足物理约束”与“正确采样后验分布”是两个不同的范畴，为科学推断提供了严谨的理论支撑。

Abstract: Generative models -- diffusion and flow matching -- are increasingly used to solve partial differential equation (PDE) inverse problems, enforcing the governing physics as a \emph{hard constraint} (via projection or guidance) and reporting the resulting samples as a Bayesian posterior with calibrated uncertainty. We show that this widely adopted recipe samples the wrong distribution. Conditioning a generative prior on a hard PDE constraint is conditioning on a measure-zero manifold -- an operation that is intrinsically ambiguous (the Borel--Kolmogorov paradox) and whose physically correct resolution, the small-residual-noise limit, carries a co-area (Fixman) Jacobian factor $[det(JJ^{\top})]^{-1/2}$ that projection- and guidance-based methods silently omit. We make the bias precise, show that it grows with the heterogeneity of the constraint sensitivity, and validate it on controlled problems against an \emph{i.i.d.} ground-truth arbiter. The omitted factor is not a second-order detail: removing it inflates the posterior error to $20\times$ the sampling-noise floor; minimal-displacement projection (as in PCFM) is biased at $9\times$ the floor; and a naive scalar reweighting does not fix it. We introduce \textbf{CoCoS}, a measure-aware constrained sampler that targets the correct co-area posterior, and show that it matches the gold-standard posterior to within sampling noise. Our results imply that ``satisfying the physics'' is not the same as ``sampling the posterior,'' and give a principled correction for uncertainty-aware scientific inference.

</details>


### [211] [Scenario Generation for Risk-Aware Reinforcement Learning with Probably Approximately Safe Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04812)
*Mohit Prashant,Arvind Easwaran*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用VAE和双重优化框架构建概率屏障证书的方法，旨在量化并缩减强化学习策略在不确定环境下的安全违规概率上下界，通过主动学习非鲁棒区域实现更可靠的安全验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 使用变分自编码器（VAE）近似状态空间的分布；2. 利用状态的潜在特征构建概率屏障证书（barrier-certificates）；3. 将其建模为双重优化问题，分别计算安全区域的上下界；4. 在上下界之间的差异区域（非鲁棒区域）进行采样训练，以持续收敛边界并提升安全保证的精确度。

Abstract: Guaranteeing safety is critical to the deployment of reinforcement learning (RL) agents in the real-world, especially as policies learned using deep RL may demonstrate susceptibility to transition perturbations that result in unknown or unsafe behaviour. A method of policy verification is to construct probabilistic barrier-certificates by sampling policy trajectories with respect to safety constraints, thereby demarcating known safe behaviour from unknown behaviour. Obtaining tight upper and lower bounds on the probability of violation of these constraints may be difficult if the policy is susceptible to transition uncertainty or perturbation that places the agent in insufficiently explored states. To address this, we approximate the distribution of the encountered state-space using a variational autoencoder (VAE) and construct upper and lower-bound barrier-certificates using latent characteristics of states to optimize for regions of known, safe behaviour with high confidence. We frame this in our work as a dual optimization problem where the lower-bound barrier-certificate presents a more conservative estimate of the safe region than the upper-bound barrier-certificate. Sampling states that lie within the set difference of the two during training, i.e. the non-robust region, allows us to tighten the upper and lower bounds to provide sharper probabilistic guarantees on safety. Within our study, we describe the guarantees placed and demonstrate the tightness of our bounds experimentally.

### [213] [Reconciling Causality and Non-Equilibrium Thermodynamics with Hamiltonian Causal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04822)
*Dario Rancati,Max Welling,Francesco Locatello*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了哈密顿因果模型（HCM），利用非平衡态热力学中的熵产生概念，解决传统因果模型在处理动态、路径依赖及非平稳物理系统时的局限性，为物理系统提供了更深层的因果推理工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的标准因果模型难以有效处理物理现象中常见的轨迹级干预、非平稳分布、路径依赖效应以及动态反馈。作者旨在弥合统计因果推理与非平衡态热力学之间的鸿沟，为复杂动态系统的因果分析提供物理基础。

Method: 提出了哈密顿因果模型（HCM），将轨迹级动力学与因果推理相结合。该模型将运动方程与可干预机制分离，通过分析系统演化过程中的路径法则差异来定义因果效应，并引入熵产生（Entropy Production）作为量化不可逆性和因果效应的核心可观测指标。

Result: 构建了一个能够处理复杂物理动态系统的因果框架；证明了熵产生能够捕捉到标准平均处理效应（ATE）在终点或累积测量中无法揭示的因果信息，从而验证了利用热力学箭头定义因果关系的有效性。

Abstract: Causal modeling of physical temporal phenomena must handle interventions that act along trajectories, nonstationary induced laws, path-dependent effects, and feedback mediated by dynamics, all challenging in standard causal models. We introduce Hamiltonian Causal Models (HCMs), a trajectory-level framework in which observed variables interact with local environments and interventions act as controls of Hamiltonian mechanisms. HCMs separate immutable equations of motion from intervenable mechanisms and define causal effects as discrepancies between interventional path laws. A key motivation for HCMs is their natural interface with non-equilibrium thermodynamics. Entropy production quantifies the irreversibility of a process and is a central causal observable: it is estimable from data and witnesses causal effects along the system's evolution that are invisible to endpoint and cumulative versions of the standard average treatment effect. As in physics, cause and effect are not primitives of the relation between two random variables but arise from the non-invertibility of the thermodynamic arrow. With this, our paper reconciles the language of statistical causal models and non-stationary thermodynamics, offering new tools to describe causality in a wide range of physical systems.

</details>


### [214] [Signed Dual Attention: Capturing Signed Dependencies in Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04833)

<details>

Result: 实验表明，该模块可以无缝集成到现有架构中，在需要符号化关系建模的任务场景下，能够显著提升模型的预测性能并保持参数的高效性。

Abstract: Initially developed for natural language processing, Transformer architectures and attention mechanisms are now central to a wide range of deep learning models, including applications in time series forecasting. A standard attention mechanism, however, implicitly assumes homophilic interactions, limiting its ability to model data with positive and negative dependencies, such as time series. In this work, we introduce the Signed Dual Attention, a novel attention formulation that captures both positive and negative relational patterns without additional parameters. By leveraging a dual message-passing scheme inspired by correlation structures, Signed Dual Attention propagates both supportive and contrastive information within a single shared block, effectively achieving the expressiveness of two head attention without additional parameters. This module can be seamlessly integrated into existing architectures and can yield performance gains in certain situations, requiring signed relational modeling. This approach opens a pathway toward more expressive and parameter-efficient transformers.

### [215] [Prediction Under Imperfect Compression: A Theory of Approximate MDL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04834)
*Qian Li,Xinyu Mao,Shang-Hua Teng,Guangxu Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了近似最小描述长度（MDL）预测的理论可靠性，证明了只要采用加性近似并满足适当的正则化条件（λ≥1），即使存在优化误差，MDL方法仍能保证序列预测的误差有界，并揭示了加性近似在理论上的核心作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的MDL预测理论要求精确优化目标函数以提供可靠的预测保证，但在实际机器学习中，通常只能进行近似优化。本文旨在探究在何种形式的近似和正则化下，近似MDL方法依然能够保证序列预测的可靠性。

Method: 本文采用了理论证明方法，特别是针对广义平衡MDL目标函数（λ·L(model)+L(data|model)），利用“亲和度伸缩”（affinity-telescoping）论证处理λ>1的情况，并使用基于精确静态MDL界限的“似然比停止”论证处理λ=1的边界情况，以分析加性近似误差下的累积期望平方预测误差。

Result: 研究证明，对于任何具有加性松弛量C的广义MDL目标函数，只要λ≥1，累积期望平方预测误差就是有限的。此外，研究还指出当0<λ<1时，系统可能发生过拟合导致累积误差无限大；且在乘性近似下，模型选择可能在所有λ>0的正则化方案中失效，证明了加性近似的必要性和充分性。

Conclusion: 本文确立了近似最小描述长度（MDL）预测框架的理论边界：加性近似误差是保证序列预测可靠性的充分必要条件。研究证明，在适当的正则化强度下（λ≥1），MDL方法对固定加性优化误差具有鲁棒性，而乘性近似则可能导致模型选择失败。

Abstract: Minimum Description Length (MDL) formalizes the principle of Occam's razor by optimizing the total description length: $L(\mathrm{model})+L(\mathrm{data} \ | \ \mathrm{model})$. For sequential prediction, the MDL method repeatedly selects a model with a minimum objective score of the observed prefix for the next step prediction. Classical MDL prediction theory shows that exact optimization of the MDL objective indeed provides a strong compression guarantee that supports reliable prediction. However, practical machine learning usually can only find models by approximately optimizing the objective function. To bridge this gap, this paper addresses the following fundamental question: Under what forms of approximation and regularization does approximate MDL still guarantee reliable sequential prediction? This work offers a principled characterization. We prove that for any approximation with additive slack $C$ of the more general form of the balanced MDL objective: $λ\cdot L(\mathrm{model})+L(\mathrm{data} \ | \ \mathrm{model})$, the cumulative expected squared prediction error is finite for all $λ\ge1$. The case $λ>1$ is proved by an affinity-telescoping argument, while the boundary case $λ=1$ is proved by a likelihood-ratio stopping argument based on exact static MDL bounds. Our results establish that classical MDL regularization remains robust to any fixed additive optimization error. Furthermore, we establish that our characterization of the approximate MDL framework is sharp: When $0<λ<1$, overfits can happen to incur infinite cumulative expected error in the universal class of estimable measures, and hence a strong form of model-complexity regularization is necessary. In addition, model selection may fail in every regularized regime $λ>0$, under multiplicative approximation, and thus, additive approximation is both sufficient and essential.

</details>


### [216] [Uncertainty-Aware End-to-End Co-Design of Neural Network Processors: From Training and Mapping to Fabrication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04850)
*Yuyang Du,Yujun Huang,Gioele Zardini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于单调协同设计理论的神经网络处理器通用框架，通过引入“置信度”作为核心优化指标，成功实现了训练、映射、制造和资源分配的解耦与模块化，显著提升了复杂系统设计的灵活性与全局优化效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经网络处理器设计通常被视为各阶段独立进行的孤立过程，或者是与特定算法深度绑定的刚性流程。这种方式导致在修改单一组件（如架构或映射策略）时，往往需要重构整个设计流水线，缺乏灵活性和全局优化能力。因此，需要一套能够解耦各设计阶段并处理系统不确定性的统一协同设计框架。

Method: 研究提出了一个由四个互操作模块组成的统一框架，涵盖神经网络训练、芯片映射、晶圆级制造及计算资源分配。该方法采用单调协同设计理论，通过定义统一的“功能-资源”接口实现模块解耦，并引入“置信度”（即成功概率的倒数）作为与成本、时间和功耗同等重要的显式优化资源。

Result: 三个案例研究验证了该框架的有效性：第一，成功在不同应用场景下恢复了帕累托最优实现；第二，证实了“置信度”可以作为一种可连续调节的设计参数进行优化；第三，证明了任一模块的优化均可自动传递至全局帕累托前沿，无需修改整体协同设计架构。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于单调协同设计理论的通用框架，能够解耦神经网络处理器设计中的各个阶段。通过引入“置信度（Confidence）”作为可优化的资源，该框架实现了各组件的独立演进与全局最优协同，为复杂硬件系统的设计提供了一种可扩展且具备鲁棒性的方法论。

Abstract: Designing a neural network processor is an end-to-end co-design problem: network architecture and training budget determine the inference workload; hardware mapping decisions determine chip area, latency, and energy; and these characteristics govern fabrication yield and manufacturing cost. In practice, these decisions are made in separate stages, and existing co-design methodologies are tightly coupled to specific algorithms, making it difficult to improve one component without reworking the entire pipeline. This paper presents a unified framework, grounded in monotone co-design theory, that composes four interoperable design blocks spanning network training, chip mapping, wafer-level fabrication, and compute resource allocation. Each block exposes only a functionality-resource interface to the rest of the system, so any block can be refined without structural changes elsewhere. A central contribution is the treatment of uncertainty: rather than collapsing stochastic outcomes into point estimates, the framework introduces Confidence, the inverse of success probability, as an explicit and optimizable resource alongside cost, time, and power. Three case studies validate the approach. The first recovers Pareto-optimal implementations across heterogeneous application scenarios. The second confirms that Confidence functions as a continuously tunable design knob rather than a post-hoc diagnostic. The third demonstrates that improving a single block's implementation set automatically propagates to the global Pareto front, without modifying the co-design diagram.

### [217] [Rethinking Incompleteness: Formalizing Protocol Divergence and Train-Once Learning for Robust IMVC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04857)
*Haolu Liu,Xiyue Wang,Xuanting Xie,Liangjian Wen,Zhao Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了缺失数据处理中“不完整性差异”的问题，证明了单一缺失率不足以描述数据完整性。为此提出了 CRAFT 模型，通过架构创新实现了一次训练、多模式推理的稳健性，显著降低了计算成本并提升了泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出传统多视图聚类（IMVC）评估范式存在缺陷，即仅关注名义缺失率而忽略了完整样本比例等结构因素，导致模型在不同缺失协议下表现差异巨大，且现有的重复训练评估模式效率低下。

Method: 提出“不完整性差异”（incompleteness divergence）概念以刻画缺失协议的结构性差异；引入 CRAFT（完整数据鲁棒注意力掩码融合 Transformer）模型，利用“样本独立性”和“掩码感知变长融合”机制，仅需在完整数据上训练一次，即可在推理时处理多样的缺失模式。

Result: 理论上证明了在完全样本比例低于特定阈值时，重建损失函数的学习变得病态；实验表明，CRAFT 在七个基准数据集上表现优于或持平现有的分配置训练基线，同时训练开销减少了 8.8 倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明，缺失数据的处理不应仅依赖于缺失率，模型的稳健性应通过架构设计（如 CRAFT）来实现，而非依赖于针对特定缺失模式的重复训练。通过将稳健性内化为架构属性，可以实现对各种缺失模式的通用性和高效性。

Abstract: Standard IMVC evaluation retrains separate models for different missing-data configurations. We show that this paradigm obscures a fundamental vulnerability: missing rate alone is insufficient to characterize data incompleteness. Specifically, we show that protocols with identical nominal missing rates can differ by up to $50\times$ in their proportion of fully observed samples, inducing drastically different learning regimes. We formalize this phenomenon as incompleteness divergence, providing measures that capture structural disparities across missing-data protocols. We further prove that for a broad class of reconstruction-based objectives, learning becomes structurally ill-posed when the proportion of complete samples falls below a critical threshold, leading to near-random performance. To bypass this theoretical bound, we propose CRAFT (Complete-data Robust Attention-masked Fusion Transformer). CRAFT shifts the burden of robustness from the loss function to the architecture via two key properties: (i) per-sample independence, which removes reliance on complete-sample co-occurrence, and (ii) mask-aware variable-length fusion, which aggregates only observed views through attention masking. This design allows a single model, trained once on complete data, to generalize to diverse missing patterns at inference time without retraining. Extensive experiments on seven benchmarks show that CRAFT matches or outperforms per-configuration baselines while reducing training overhead by $8.8\times$, demonstrating that robustness to missing data can be achieved as an inherent architectural property. Code (CRAFT) and our imvc-audit toolkit are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/CRAFT-BF80/ and https://anonymous.4open.science/r/imvc-audit-8263/.

</details>


### [218] [Learning Empirically Admissible Neural Heuristics for Combinatorial Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04860)
*Siddharth Sahay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于组合谜题求解的新型神经网络启发式方法。通过改进训练目标（可采纳贝尔曼算子与非对称损失）和事后校准技术，有效解决了深度学习启发式函数的“过估计”问题，在保证最优路径搜索的同时，大幅提升了搜索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 启发式搜索算法（如A*）要保证路径最优性，必须使用可采纳的启发式函数（即不产生过高估计）。然而，现有的深度强化学习方法（如DeepCubeA）通常使用均方误差（MSE）训练，这会导致启发式函数产生过估计，从而破坏搜索的最优性保证。因此，亟需一种能够学习出既准确又具备严格可采纳性的神经网络启发式函数的方法。

Method: 1. 提出“可采纳贝尔曼算子”（Admissible Bellman Operator），通过约束值函数的更新过程来强制执行下限估计；2. 采用“非对称损失函数”（Asymmetric Loss），对过估计行为进行严厉惩罚；3. 设计“事后校准安全偏移”（Post-hoc calibration safety offset），在验证集上计算并修正残余的函数逼近误差，确保启发式的绝对可采纳性。

Result: 实验表明，所提出的校准神经网络启发式方法在测试过程中未出现任何可采纳性违规。在保持路径最优性的前提下，相比标准解析基准，该方法在2x2魔方、3x3 Lights Out以及8-Puzzle谜题上的搜索节点展开数分别减少了83.0%、19.9%和1.9%。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入验证校准的可采纳性神经网络启发式方法，成功解决了深度强化学习中启发式函数过度估计导致的最优路径搜索失败问题。该方法在保证搜索结果最优性的同时，显著提升了搜索效率，证明了将机器学习与形式化可采纳性约束结合的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Finding optimal solution paths for combinatorial puzzles like the Rubik's Cube, sliding tile puzzles, and Lights Out remains a classical challenge in artificial intelligence. Heuristic search algorithms, such as A* , guarantee path optimality only when using an admissible heuristic-one that never overestimates the true remaining cost-to-go. Deep reinforcement learning (RL) methods like DeepCubeA train deep neural networks to approximate cost-to-go heuristics. However, standard mean-squared error (MSE) training regularly yields overestimations, violating admissibility and compromising solution optimality. In this paper, we introduce a generalizable framework for learning validation-calibrated admissible neural heuristics. We train a value network using an underestimating Admissible Bellman Operator combined with an Asymmetric Loss function to penalize overestimation. To account for residual neural function approximation errors, we propose a post-hoc calibration safety offset computed over validation scrambles. We demonstrate that our calibrated neural heuristics achieve no observed admissibility violations under the evaluation protocol and preserve path optimality in practice while reducing search node expansions by up to 83.0% on a 2 by 2 Rubik's Cube, 19.9% on a 3 by 3 Lights Out grid, and 1.9% on an 8-Puzzle compared to standard analytical baselines.

Method: 采用固定预算最优臂识别（fixed-budget best-arm identification）的理论框架，通过将先验直接建模为配置性能的分布，推导出了依赖于分布的样本复杂度界限，并对多保真度HPO进行了形式化分析。

Abstract: Large-scale hyperparameter optimization (HPO) in automated machine learning (AutoML) consumes substantial computational resources, raising growing concerns about scalability and energy efficiency. Existing methods use prior information heuristically to accelerate both black-box and multi-fidelity settings, but they lack a characterization of how prior informativeness quantitatively reduces sample complexity. In this work, we provide the first distribution-dependent sample complexity bounds for multi-fidelity HPO with priors through the formal lens of fixed-budget best-arm identification. By modeling priors directly over arm means as configuration performance, we derive explicit, distribution-dependent error bounds that quantify the relationship between priors and evaluation budget. Our analysis shows that informative priors, which concentrate probability mass on near-optimal arms, yield reductions in the number of required evaluations, whereas baseline performance is recovered with uninformative or misleading priors. We conduct proof-of-concept experiments on a synthetic benchmark and on LCBench, a common multi-fidelity HPO benchmark for deep learning, to confirm our theoretical results, achieving up to 90% budget reduction while retaining solution quality.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Tabular foundation models, such as TabPFN, achieve strong performance on tabular datasets with numerical and categorical data, but do not natively handle high-cardinality text features. Standard pipelines, therefore, embed text with a language model and compress the resulting vectors with PCA into a small number of scalar features before inputting them into TabPFN. This creates an information bottleneck: most embedding dimensions are discarded, and the compressed representation must then be expanded again by TabPFN's feature encoder. End-to-end alternatives can avoid PCA, but they require large amounts of pretraining data containing text cells and usually perform subpar compared to tabular foundation models that were pretrained on large amounts of synthetic data. Inspired by modality-alignment approaches like LLaVA (vision-to-LLM token projection) and TableGPT-style systems (table-to-LLM token projection), we introduce the TabPFN Text Adapter (text-to-TFM token projection). We freeze both the sentence encoder and TabPFN, and train only a lightweight adapter that maps text embeddings into a short sequence of tokens in TabPFN's embedding space. This design removes the PCA bottleneck, preserves TabPFN's numerical strengths, and is more efficient to train than end-to-end text-tabular pipelines.

### [221] [Worker Utility as Hysteresis: A Preisach Model of Transaction Acceptance in Gig Labour Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04916)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零工经济中工人的效用不可直接观测，仅能观测到接受或拒绝的二元结果。现有的模型往往忽略了劳动供给行为中典型的滞后效应（即价格涨跌对接受率的非对称影响），导致无法准确评估工人的保留工资，进而限制了薪酬定价的优化空间。

Method: 研究提出了基于Preisach滞后算子的建模方法：1. 采用双输出神经网络分别拟合接受效用U1(X)和拒绝效用U0(X)；2. 将Preisach间隙（U1-U0）与价格阈值编码作为特征，利用XGBoost进行分类；3. 利用价格对阈值编码（price-to-threshold encoding）来捕捉工人的非对称性响应行为。

Result: 在36,891笔交易数据上，该模型达到了0.827的Jaccard系数和0.799的ROC AUC。通过该模型进行定价优化，可在将工资总额降低21.3%的同时，使预期成交率提升9.7个百分点，证明了考虑滞后效应对于提升平台经济效率的重要性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了Preisach滞后模型是表征零工经济中工人潜伏偏好的有效框架。通过引入明确的无差异区域（Indifference Zone），该模型能够同时识别出可以通过降薪实现成本节约的交易以及通过适度涨薪显著提高达成率的交易，从而实现了劳动力成本优化与履约率提升的双重目标。

Abstract: Worker utility is not observed -- only its consequence is. Each gig transaction produces a single bit: accepted or rejected. We argue this structure points directly to the Preisach hysteresis model as the natural representation of latent worker preferences. The Preisach operator models aggregate output as an integral over a population of binary threshold elements -- precisely the structure that emerges when heterogeneous workers each carry a private acceptance wage. We estimate two latent utility surfaces: acceptance utility U_1(X) and rejection utility U_0(X), via a dual-output neural network (shared layers 256->128, margin loss enforcing U_1 >= U_0). Classification reduces to the Preisach gap U_1(X) - U_0(X), passed into an XGBoost classifier alongside clip-stabilised price-to-threshold encodings. On 36,891 gig transactions, this pipeline achieves Jaccard = 0.827 and ROC AUC = 0.799. The price-to-threshold encoding accounts for +11.0 pp AUC over raw utility features. The model confirms the directional asymmetry hysteresis predicts: price decreases depress completion rates more than equivalent increases raise them. Applied to the full dataset, the model's recommendations simultaneously reduce the total wage bill by 21.3% and increase expected fill rate by 9.7 pp. For 74.2% of transactions, P(accept) already exceeds 0.80; reducing the wage keeps it above threshold (mean post-cut P = 0.972), releasing cost savings (median 31%). For the remaining 25.4%, a median 7% wage increase recovers +43 pp acceptance. A model without an explicit indifference zone cannot execute both moves simultaneously.

</details>


### [222] [AdaKoop: Efficient Modeling of Nonlinear Dynamics from Nonstationary Data Streams with Koopman Operator Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04930)
*Naoki Chihara,Ren Fujiwara,Yasuko Matsubara,Yasushi Sakurai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AdaKoop 是一种基于 Koopman 算子理论的高效流式算法，通过将非线性动力学线性化并引入自适应更新机制，实现了对非平稳数据流中复杂模式的快速、准确建模，显著提升了实时分析的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实时数据流分析中，如何高效且准确地捕捉非平稳数据流中的非线性动态模式是一个重大挑战。现有的非线性建模方法往往面临计算复杂度过高的问题，难以满足实时处理的严格时效性要求，因此需要一种既能保持计算可控性，又能准确拟合非线性动力学的算法。

Method: 本研究提出了 AdaKoop 算法，主要包含以下核心方法：1. 利用 Koopman 算子理论，将复杂的非线性动力学通过有限维逼近转化为高维空间中的线性演化；2. 构建双视角概率框架，将原始观测和再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）特征建模为潜变量的发射，从而避开了耗时的非线性优化；3. 结合统计假设检验机制，动态监测数据流的模式转换，并结合增量更新策略，以适应非平稳数据的持续变化。

Result: 在 71 个跨领域的实际基准数据集上的实验结果表明，AdaKoop 在实时预测精度和计算效率方面均优于现有的先进方法，证明了其处理非平稳数据流的优越性与实用性。

Conclusion: AdaKoop 通过将复杂的非线性动力学转化为线性系统，成功解决了实时数据流分析中的计算效率与精度之间的权衡问题。该方法证明了 Koopman 算子理论在处理非平稳非线性动态系统中的强大潜力，为实时建模提供了一个高效且稳健的框架。

Abstract: Real-time data analysis requires the ability to accurately and adaptively address nonlinear dynamics in a nonstationary data stream while preserving computational efficiency. However, nonlinear dynamics are so complex that capturing dynamically changing nonlinear patterns and utilizing them for downstream tasks under strict time constraints is nontrivial. To bridge the gap between nonlinear complexity and computational tractability, this study applies Koopman operator theory, which states that nonlinear dynamics can be represented as linear transitions in an infinite-dimensional space. Building upon finite-dimensional approximations of this operator, we present AdaKoop, an efficient streaming algorithm for modeling nonlinear dynamics over nonstationary data streams. Our approach utilizes a probabilistic framework grounded in Koopman operator theory, treating both raw observations and reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS) features as emissions from latent vectors. This dual-view formulation allows nonlinear dynamics to be expressed as a tractable linear system. Therefore, AdaKoop enables the efficient and stable modeling of nonlinear dynamics in a streaming fashion, avoiding the prohibitive computational costs of iterative nonlinear optimization. Furthermore, to address nonstationarity in data streams, AdaKoop adaptively detects the switching of patterns via statistical hypothesis testing for abrupt pattern shifts and incrementally updates model parameters to handle continuous changes. Extensive experiments on a total of 71 practical benchmark datasets across various domains demonstrate that AdaKoop outperforms state-of-the-art methods in terms of real-time forecasting accuracy and computational efficiency.

</details>


### [223] [Toward Multi-Domain and Long-Tailed Quantization via Feature Alignment and Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04920)
*Chin-Yuan Yeh,Ting-An Chen,De-Nian Yang,Ming-Syan Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度神经网络量化方法大多针对单领域且类别平衡的数据，在面对现实中普遍存在的领域偏移（Domain Shift）和严重类别不平衡（Class Imbalance）问题时表现不佳。

Conclusion: EmaQ 和 EmaQ-LT 为在复杂现实场景（如多领域偏移和严重类别不平衡）下进行模型量化提供了有效且鲁棒的解决方案，证明了通过分布对齐和针对性偏差修正可以显著提升低比特量化模型的泛化能力。

Abstract: Quantizing deep neural networks is essential for efficient inference on resource-constrained devices. However, most existing methods are designed for single-domain and class-balanced data, leaving practical settings with domain shifts or severe class imbalance underexplored. We address these challenges with Efficient Multi-Domain Alignment Quantization (EmaQ), which aligns domain distributions through a CDF-based projection and uses sensitivity-aware weight aggregation to stabilize multi-domain quantization. We further extend EmaQ to EmaQ-LT for long-tailed quantization by introducing class-conditioned variance scaling and confidence-based logit adjustment to mitigate majority-class overconfidence. Theoretical analyses establish convergence guarantees and motivate the proposed sensitivity and scaling mechanisms. Experiments on standard, multi-domain (Office-31, Digits), and long-tailed (SynDigits-LT, CIFAR-10-LT, CIFAR-100-LT) benchmarks show that EmaQ and EmaQ-LT achieve strong low-bit performance under domain shift and class imbalance.

### [224] [Invariant Gradient Alignment for Robust Reasoning Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05025)
*Zehua Cheng,Wei Dai,Jiahao Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型在不同语义但逻辑相似的输入下泛化能力差的问题，本文提出了IGA框架，通过对齐不同领域的梯度更新，显著提升了模型的逻辑推理稳健性和跨领域泛化表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）存在“捷径学习”问题，即当输入语义表面与训练数据不同但逻辑结构相同时，模型常会失效。这种缺陷削弱了将思维链推理能力从教师模型蒸馏到较小模型的效果。

Method: 提出了一种名为“不变梯度对齐”（Invariant Gradient Alignment, IGA）的训练框架，包含三个核心创新点：1. 构建逻辑异构集，即跨不同语义领域共享相同逻辑结构的问题组；2. 使用可微连续梯度冲突掩码，抑制跨领域梯度的高方差维度，保留不变方向；3. 通过截断SVD投影将掩码梯度映射回LoRA低秩流形，确保参数高效性。

Result: 在四个基准测试中，IGA的表现优于八个基线模型，准确率较ERM-SFT提升高达14.3个百分点；逻辑一致性分数从0.142降至0.031，表征不变性提升了四倍，且在理论上证明了其比经验风险最小化（ERM）具有更紧的OOD泛化界。

Conclusion: IGA通过在不同领域间对齐梯度，有效缓解了大型语言模型在OOD场景下的捷径学习问题，显著提升了模型在逻辑推理任务中的稳健性和跨领域泛化能力，为知识蒸馏提供了更可靠的路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) suffer from shortcut learning: they systematically fail on out-of-distribution (OOD) inputs whose semantic surface differs from training data, even when the logical structure is identical. This undermines knowledge distillation pipelines that transfer chain-of-thought reasoning to smaller students. We introduce Invariant Gradient Alignment (IGA), a training framework that aligns gradient updates across semantically diverse but logically isomorphic examples via three innovations: (i) Logical Isomer Sets, groups of problems sharing identical logical structure across distinct semantic domains (mathematics, medicine, law, science); (ii) a differentiable \emph{Continuous Gradient Conflict Mask}, that suppresses parameter dimensions with high cross-domain gradient variance while preserving invariant directions; and (iii) a truncated SVD projection of the masked gradient back onto the LoRA low-rank manifold, maintaining parameter efficiency throughout. Theoretically, IGA yields tighter OOD generalization bounds than ERM, scaling with the number of isomer domains, and converges at the standard SGD rate under mild regularity. Empirically, IGA outperforms eight baselines across four benchmarks with accuracy gains up to 14.3 pp over ERM-SFT and a Logical Consistency Score of 0.031 versus 0.142 -- a fourfold improvement in representational invariance.

### [225] [Sequential Data Poisoning in LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04929)
*Jack Sanderson,Yihan Wang,Xiaoqian Lu,Gautam Kamath,Yiwei Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大语言模型后训练阶段中被忽视的“序列数据投毒”威胁，证明了攻击者可以通过跨阶段协同合作，利用单一阶段分析无法发现的复合漏洞来操控模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文献通常假设大模型后训练的各个阶段（SFT、RLHF/DPO）是相互独立的，并分别评估其安全性，但忽略了多阶段协同攻击的可能性。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过研究全流程的信任问题，揭示被现有评估体系所忽视的复合型漏洞。

Method: 研究提出了“序列数据投毒”威胁模型，旨在分析多个攻击者如何分别在监督微调（SFT）和偏好优化（如DPO、PPO）阶段注入投毒数据。研究通过实验对比了单一阶段投毒与跨阶段协同投毒的效果，验证了攻击策略在不同管线中的协同机制。

Result: 实验结果表明，在SFT转DPO的管线中，跨阶段的攻击效果具有累加性，分摊投毒预算比集中在单一阶段更有效；在SFT转PPO的管线中，攻击效果具有互补性，即便单一阶段的攻击无效，组合攻击仍能成功操控模型。这些结果证实了当前针对独立阶段的安全性分析往往会系统性地低估复合漏洞。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型后训练阶段中存在的“单一攻击者错觉”。研究表明，仅针对单一阶段进行安全性评估会严重低估潜在威胁，因为攻击者可以通过在不同阶段协同作案，产生累加或互补的危害效应。这强调了在评估大模型安全时，必须采用端到端的全流程视角。

Abstract: LLM post-training proceeds through multiple stages, e.g., supervised fine-tuning (SFT) followed by reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) or direct preference optimization (DPO), where each stage draws data from different, potentially untrusted sources. Existing literature assumes data poisoning attacks may occur at each training stage, but neglects the possibility of multiple attackers. To study the trustworthiness of the entire post-training pipeline, we propose the threat model of sequential data poisoning, where multiple adversaries separately poison the SFT and preference datasets. Under this threat model, we identify the single-attacker illusion: each adversary, evaluated in isolation, appears to pose a negligible threat. Yet when adversaries collaborate across stages, the true vulnerability is revealed. In the SFT $\to$ DPO pipeline, their contributions are additive: splitting a fixed poison budget across stages outperforms concentrating it in either stage alone. In the SFT $\to$ PPO pipeline, their contributions are complementary: neither SFT nor reward model poisoning succeeds individually, yet their combination does. These findings show that security analyses of individual post-training stages systematically underestimate compound vulnerabilities that emerge only from their interaction. Code is available at https://github.com/jcksanderson/sequential-poisoning.

</details>


### [226] [Mean-based algorithms: A lower bound and regret](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04931)
*Julius Durmann,Amelie Kleber*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入研究了赌博机反馈下均值算法的性能限制，提出了适用于未知时间跨度的新型均值算法，并从理论上证明了均值算法与无遗憾算法之间存在交集，从而在收敛速度与算法属性之间建立了更明确的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均值算法在经济博弈中能收敛至近似纳什均衡的策略，具有良好的理论属性。然而，在赌博机反馈（bandit-feedback）场景下，相较于成熟的算法，其收敛速度较慢且缺乏关于未知时间跨度设置下的理论边界。本文旨在填补这些理论空白，并评估其在实际任务中的表现。

Method: 1. 推导了定义均值算法的序列 $\gamma_t$ 的理论下界，确立了其学习速率的极限；2. 提出了两种针对未知时间跨度的改进均值算法：一种是 $\epsilon$-greedy 的推广，另一种是对均值化 Exp3 的扩展；3. 通过实验评估了这些算法的性能；4. 对比分析了均值算法与无遗憾算法之间的数学关系。

Result: 研究确立了 $\gamma_t$ 的下界，揭示了算法学习速度的限制。所提出的新型均值算法在实验中表现出与现有主流赌博机算法相当的竞争力。此外，证明了均值算法类与无遗憾算法类之间存在重叠，为理解此类算法的可利用性提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: 均值算法在未知时间跨度和仅有赌博机反馈的条件下是可行且具有竞争力的。研究揭示了均值算法与无遗憾算法之间存在非平凡的交集，证明了同时具备均值特性和无遗憾特性的算法是存在的，从而深化了对该类算法可利用性的理论理解。

Abstract: Mean-based algorithms are a class of online learning algorithms that assign low probability to actions with low average rewards. Recent work indicates these algorithms converge favorably to serially undominated actions, which approximate Nash equilibria in economic games. However, empirical studies also show slower convergence compared to established algorithms in bandit-feedback scenarios.
  We study mean-based algorithms when the time horizon is unknown and only bandit feedback is available. In this setting, we provide the first lower bound on the algorithm-defining sequence $γ_t$ that formally establishes a limit on how fast these algorithms can learn. Additionally, we propose two mean-based algorithms: one generalizes $ε$-greedy, and the other extends the mean-based Exp3 to unknown horizons. Our experiments show that mean-based algorithms, although slightly slower, can perform competitively with other bandit-feedback algorithms.
  We further analyze the relationship to no-regret algorithms. Depending on the choice of $γ_t$, the intersection with no-regret algorithms is non-trivial, and we show that algorithms exist that are both mean-based and no-regret. This adds context to the "exploitability" of this class of algorithms that previous contributions suggest.

### [227] [Towards Efficient and Evidence-grounded Mobility Prediction with LLM-Driven Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05130)
*Linyao Chen,Qinlao Zhao,Zechen Li,Mingming Li,Likun Ni,Jinyu Chen,Yuhao Yao,Xuan Song,Noboru Koshizuka,Hiroki Kobayashi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在三个数据集上测试表明，AgentMob在无需训练的LLM方法中表现最佳；在处理非“快路径”（即模糊）情况时，AgentMob通过自适应证据收集，将预测准确率从基线的30.65%提升至48.62%。

Conclusion: AgentMob框架证明了通过代理（Agent）架构实现自适应证据收集，能够显著提升大语言模型在处理复杂且模棱两可的个体移动预测任务中的准确性，且无需进行昂贵的模型微调。

Abstract: Individual-level mobility prediction is central to urban simulation, transportation planning, and policy analysis. Supervised sequence models achieve strong accuracy but require task-specific training and offer limited decision-level transparency. Recent LLM-based methods improve interpretability, yet mostly rely on static prompts and single-pass inference, limiting their ability to seek additional evidence when mobility signals are weak or conflicting. We propose \method{}, a training-free LLM-driven agent framework that formulates next-location prediction as adaptive evidence-controlled decision making. \method{} resolves routine cases through a fast path based on historical regularity, while ambiguous cases trigger iterative tool use over recent trajectories, historical behavior, stay-move likelihood, and geographical evidence. Across three mobility datasets, AgentMob achieves the strongest overall performance among training-free LLM-based methods, with GPT-5.4 reaching 71.42\% Acc@1 on BW, 33.14\% on YJMob100K, and 33.50\% on Shanghai ISP. On BW non-fast-path cases, the LLM controller improves Acc@1 from 30.65\% to 48.62\% over a same-tool statistical baseline, showing that its main benefit lies in resolving ambiguous predictions through adaptive evidence gathering. Our code is available at https://github.com/Unknown-zoo/AgentMob.

### [228] [STaR-Quant: State-Time Consistent Post-Training Quantization for Diffusion Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04945)
*Xin Yan,Aqiang Wang,Zhenglin Wan,Xingrui Yuand Ivor Tsang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了针对扩散大语言模型（DLLM）的 STaR-Quant 量化框架，通过解决去噪过程中的激活分布偏移和误差累积问题，有效提升了模型在低比特下的运行效率与精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大语言模型（DLLM）虽具备双向上下文优势，但由于其巨大的模型参数和迭代去噪机制，导致计算和显存开销巨大。现有的低比特量化方法在处理 DLLM 时，未充分考虑去噪过程中特殊的激活分布差异及迭代步骤带来的误差累积，导致模型性能下降。

Method: STaR-Quant 框架提出了两项核心技术：1) 状态引导激活转换 (SGAT)，通过统一的权重变换与针对掩码/非掩码令牌的差异化激活映射，解决激活分布不一致问题；2) 时间注意力补偿 (TAC)，利用轻量级块对角仿射映射校正迭代去噪过程中的量化注意力误差。

Result: 实验表明，STaR-Quant 在保持量化精度的前提下，显著优于现有的强基准线算法。该方法在低比特权重与激活量化配置下，实现了最高 1.69 倍的加速和 3.14 倍的显存节省。

Conclusion: STaR-Quant 是一种有效的扩散大语言模型（DLLM）后训练量化框架，通过针对性处理状态依赖的激活差异和时间步间的误差积累，成功在低比特量化下实现了显著的推理加速与显存优化，为高效部署 DLLM 提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (DLLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive LLMs by generating text through iterative masked denoising with bidirectional context. However, their large model sizes and iterative denoising process introduce substantial memory and computational overhead, motivating post-training quantization for efficient deployment. In this paper, we identify two key challenges for low-bit DLLM quantization: state-dependent activation disparity and temporal error accumulation. Masked and unmasked tokens exhibit different activation distributions within each denoising step, while quantization errors can accumulate across steps during iterative decoding. To address these challenges, we propose STaR-Quant, a state-time consistent PTQ framework for DLLMs. STaR-Quant introduces State-Guided Activation Transformation (SGAT) to assign masked and unmasked tokens to different activation transformation spaces with a unified static weight-side transformation. It further introduces Temporal Attention Compensation (TAC) to correct the quantized attention representation via a lightweight block-diagonal affine mapping. Experiments on representative DLLMs demonstrate that STaR-Quant consistently improves low-bit weight-activation quantization over strong PTQ baselines, while delivering up to 1.69x speedup and 3.14x memory saving over FP16 deployment.

</details>


### [229] [Be Fair! Can Machine Learning Engineering Agents Adhere to Fairness Constraints?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04971)
*Anna Richter,Julia Stoyanovich,Sebastian Schelter*

TL;DR: 本文指出了现有MLE智能体在敏感领域缺乏责任评估机制的问题，通过皮肤癌分类案例研究发现，当前智能体在公平性和质量上远未达到人工基准，亟需构建可由人类监管的负责任智能体开发框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着MLE智能体在自动化端到端机器学习流程中的应用，在敏感和受监管领域出现了“责任缺口”。现有的基准测试无法有效评估智能体在模型正确性、稳健性、公平性和合规性方面的表现，限制了其在专业领域的安全应用。

Method: 1. 提出了以“责任”为中心的评估框架需求（Desiderata）；2. 选取黑色素瘤分类作为案例研究，将不同肤色的公平性作为关键责任约束；3. 对两款主流MLE智能体生成的管道进行实证评估，并与专家手动设计的基准进行对比。

Result: 实验结果显示，MLE智能体生成的管道表现出较高的不确定性（高方差），且在预测质量和公平性指标上，即便经过公平性导向的提示，仍持续低于专家手动设计的基准模型。

Conclusion: 目前的机器学习工程（MLE）智能体在处理敏感和受监管任务时表现不足。研究表明，需要重新设计这些智能体，以实现人机协作，确保人类能够引导搜索过程，并可靠地评估生成流程的合规性和质量。

Abstract: Machine learning engineering (MLE) agents promise to automate end-to-end ML pipeline development from raw data and natural language instructions, potentially making ML accessible to non-technical domain experts. However, in sensitive and regulated domains, this abstraction creates a responsibility gap: end-users may lack visibility into design choices that affect correctness, robustness, fairness, and regulatory compliance. We argue that existing benchmarks are insufficient to assess whether MLE agents can be safely applied in such settings. We propose desiderata for a responsibility-centered evaluation framework and conduct an exploratory study on melanoma classification, focusing on fairness across skin tones as a responsibility constraint. When evaluating two recent MLE agents, we find that agent-generated pipelines show high variance and consistently underperform manually designed baselines in both predictive quality and fairness, despite fairness-oriented prompts. These preliminary results suggest that further research is needed towards redesigning MLE agents to allow humans to guide the search process and reliably assess the compliance and quality of the generated ML pipelines.

### [230] [AlphaQ: Calibration-Free Bit Allocation for Mixture-of-Experts Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04980)
*Wanqi Yang,Yuexiao Ma,Alexander Conzelmann,Xiawu Zheng,Michael W. Mahoney,T. Konstantin Rusch,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AlphaQ 是一种无需校准数据的 MoE 模型量化方法，它利用重尾自正则化（HT-SR）理论，通过分析专家权重矩阵的谱特征来动态分配量化位宽，在显著降低模型内存占用的同时，保持了极高的模型精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 MoE 模型量化方法通常依赖校准数据来评估专家重要性并决定位宽分配，但对于前沿的 MoE 大模型，原始训练数据往往是私有的，导致校准集成为不完美的代理，造成专家利用率评估偏差和次优的量化方案。因此，亟需一种无需依赖特定校准数据的、能够有效区分专家重要性的量化策略。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 AlphaQ 的无需校准（calibration-free）的 MoE 量化方法。该方法基于重尾自正则化（HT-SR）理论，通过分析专家权重矩阵的谱特性来评估其“训练质量”：谱表现出更强重尾特征的专家被认为质量更高，应分配更高的比特位宽；反之则可以更激进地量化。最终通过求解一个以总比特预算为约束的优化问题，实现最优的位宽分配。

Result: 在多个 MoE 模型上的实验结果表明，AlphaQ 在匹配的位宽预算下表现优于现有的校准驱动基准方法。特别是在 Qwen1.5-MoE 模型上，AlphaQ 在平均仅 3.5 位比特的专家精度下实现了接近全精度的表现，并提供了超过 4 倍的内存压缩。

Conclusion: AlphaQ 证明了基于权重矩阵谱特性的无校准量化方法在 MoE 模型中是高度有效的。通过利用重尾自正则化（HT-SR）理论，该方法在无需原始训练数据的情况下，能够实现优于传统数据依赖型方法的压缩效果，为大规模 MoE 模型的部署提供了更高效、更具鲁棒性的解决方案。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures scale model capacity through sparse expert activation, but their deployment remains memory-bound because all expert weights must reside in memory. Mixed-precision quantization can substantially reduce this footprint by assigning different bit-widths to different experts. Existing approaches, however, typically rely on calibration data to estimate expert importance and determine bit allocation. For frontier MoE LLMs, the original training data, and hence the true training distribution, is proprietary and inaccessible. As a result, calibration sets are inevitably imperfect surrogates, and this can misestimate expert utilization and lead to suboptimal bit allocation. Motivated by the substantial cross-expert quality variability observed in modern MoE models, and by the success of Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory at predicting neural network model quality without access to training or testing data, we propose AlphaQ, a calibration-free bit-allocation method for MoE quantization. AlphaQ draws on HT-SR theory and follows a simple principle: experts with more heavy-tailed weight spectra are typically better trained and hence should receive higher bit-widths, while experts with weaker heavy-tailed structure can be quantized more aggressively. AlphaQ operationalizes this principle by measuring expert-wise spectral heavy-tailedness and solving a budget-constrained optimization problem that minimizes total quantization error under a global bit-budget constraint. Across several MoE models, AlphaQ consistently outperforms calibration-based baselines under matched bit budgets. Notably, on Qwen1.5-MoE, AlphaQ achieves near full-precision accuracy with an average expert precision of only 3.5 bits, while delivering more than 4$\times$ memory compression. Our code is available at https://github.com/Superone77/AlphaQ.

</details>

Method: 构建了两类互补的TCR-抗原基准数据集，旨在解决当前模型评估中缺乏严谨测试集的问题，从而实现对比对模型性能和泛化能力的无偏评估。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 引入“行动推断（Action Inference）”机制：允许智能体预测其他智能体的动作意图，以提高自身策略的准确性与稳定性。2. 改进经验回放：采用基于几何分布的加权重要性采样策略，赋予近期及更具信息量的经验更高的优先级，从而缓解多智能体环境中的非平稳性问题。

Result: 在PettingZoo的Predator-Prey任务实验表明：行动推断机制显著提升了学习稳定性及智能体间的协作水平；基于几何分布的重要性采样极大地提高了算法的探索效率，优于标准MADDPG算法。

Abstract: We investigate multi-agent deep reinforcement learning and propose two enhancements to the Multi-Agent Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (MADDPG) algorithm. First, we introduce a novel Action Inference mechanism that enables each agent to predict other agents' intended actions, thereby improving the accuracy and stability of its own policy. Second, we apply an importance sampling strategy, using geometric distribution, in the replay buffer to prioritize more recent and informative experiences, which helps mitigate the non-stationarity inherent in multi-agent environments. We evaluate both modifications on the discrete-action Predator-Prey task provided by the PettingZoo library, a flexible Python interface for general multi-agent reinforcement learning benchmarks. Our results indicate that Action Inference is effective in improving learning stability and inter-agent cooperation and that importance sampling using geometric distribution can lead to significant improvements in exploration efficiency over standard MADDPG. Code available at https://github.com/shaashwathsivakumar/MARL_Proj

### [233] [Graph Cascades: Contagion-Based Mesoscopic Rewiring for Structure-Aware Graph Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05046)
*Meher Chaitanya,My Le,Luana Ruiz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Graph Cascades 策略，通过在 O(|V|+|E|) 时间内利用多跳强化过程构建辅助图，有效捕捉中尺度结构，从而显著提升各类图神经网络在异质性和中高度图上的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图神经网络和 Transformer 通常仅关注局部邻域或全局注意力，忽略了介于两者之间的中尺度图结构信息。研究者旨在通过一种高效的重连策略，增强模型捕捉这种中尺度结构的能力，以改善在不同同质性/异质性图上的表现。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Graph Cascades 的中尺度图重连策略。该方法基于传染扩散过程（contagion-based diffusion processes），在 O(|V|+|E|) 时间复杂度内构建辅助图，将具有多跳强化特征的节点对提升为直接邻居，从而超越了纯局部边或全局注意力机制。

Result: 实验表明，Graph Cascades 在节点分类基准测试中提升了多种 GNN 和稀疏 GT 主干网络的性能，特别是在异质性图和中高度图上表现优异。此外，研究还通过理论和实验验证了该方法在低度规则图及存在结构瓶颈的图上的局限性，证实了其性能与重连图的结构特性紧密相关。

Conclusion: Graph Cascades 提供了一种高效且具有理论支撑的图重连策略，能够通过捕捉中尺度结构显著提升 GNN 和 GT 的性能。研究同时明确了该方法的适用边界，为理解图结构与模型性能之间的关系提供了重要洞察。

Abstract: We introduce Graph Cascades, a mesoscopic rewiring strategy for Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) and Graph Transformers (GTs) that captures intermediate-scale graph structure beyond purely local edges or fully global attention. Using contagion-based diffusion processes, Graph Cascades constructs, in O(|V|+|E|) time, an auxiliary graph where node pairs supported by repeated multi-hop reinforcement are promoted to direct neighbors. We theoretically characterize when reinforcement-based rewiring helps: sufficient conditions under which reinforcement-based edge selection is more label-aligned than direct adjacency, an SBM witness in which two-hop reinforcement is perfectly homophilic, and a formalization of mesoscopic connectivity via graph effective resistance. Empirically, across node-classification benchmarks, Graph Cascades improves multiple GNN and sparse-GT backbones, with the most reliable gains observed on heterophilic and moderate- to high-degree homophilic graphs. The theoretical conditions also identify regimes where mesoscopic rewiring is unlikely to be beneficial -- low-degree regular graphs and graphs with structural bottlenecks -- and these predictions match the observed failures. We additionally observe tight correlations between performance and structural properties in the rewired graphs.

### [234] [FLAGG: Flexible Autoregressive Graph Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05067)
*Samuel Cognolato,Alessandro Sperduti,Luciano Serafini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为FLAGG的图生成框架，通过将一次性生成模型转化为自回归生成过程，有效克服了传统图生成方法在处理不同规模图时的局限性，显著提升了图生成的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图生成模型主要分为一次性生成和自回归生成两类，前者难以处理大规模图，后者在处理小规模图时表现欠佳。为了克服这两类方法的局限性，作者旨在构建一个能够灵活结合两种模式的统一框架，以适应不同规模和拓扑结构的图生成任务。

Method: 提出了FLAGG（灵活自回归图生成）框架。该方法将图生成过程分解为多个一次性生成步骤的序列：首先通过随机节点移除过程定义序列策略，随后训练一个“插入模型（Insertion Model）”来学习并反转该移除过程，从而实现逐步生成图的结构。此框架具有高度的模块化，可集成各种现有的一次性生成模型。

Result: 在多个不同规模和领域的图数据集上进行的实验表明，FLAGG框架在采样质量方面均优于现有的单次性生成基准和自回归基准模型，验证了该方法在提升图生成性能方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的FLAGG框架成功结合了一次性（one-shot）和自回归（sequential）图生成模型的优势。通过引入随机节点移除过程及相应的插入模型，实现了对图生成的灵活控制，为处理不同规模和拓扑结构的图数据提供了一种更具通用性和高效性的解决方案。

Abstract: The Deep Graph Generation's panorama spans two extremes: one-shot and sequential models. The former generates nodes and edges jointly, while the latter samples them autoregressively. Each method performs better in different graph domains depending on size and topology, but neither is applicable to all graph categories. For instance, one-shot methods struggle with generating large graphs, while sequential methods underperform on smaller graphs. A possible way to overcome these limitations is to flexibly combine the two methods in a unique system. In this work, we propose the FLAGG (Flexible Autoregressive Graph Generation) framework, which sequentially generates portions of graphs with one-shot models. FLAGG can apply any one-shot model to make it autoregressive, allowing flexibility in choosing the sequential policy. This policy is specified through a stochastic node removal process, which an Insertion Model learns to reverse. We evaluate FLAGG with the DiGress one-shot model on several data sets of different graph sizes and domains. We show that the approach outperforms both one-shot and autoregressive baselines in terms of sampling quality.

### [235] [RIDE: An Open Dataset and Benchmark for Train Delay Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05070)

Abstract: Train delay prediction is an important problem for both passengers and railway operators, yet progress in the field remains difficult to assess due to the lack of standardized datasets, prediction targets, and evaluation protocols. To address this gap, we introduce RIDE, an open dataset and benchmark for train delay prediction built at nationwide scale over the Belgian railway network. RIDE covers 94.5M train events, 3.6M journeys, and 35.7M weather records from 2023 to 2025. It is organized as a layered data pipeline from raw railway and weather sources to two public releases: a reusable intermediate relational dataset and model-ready benchmark datasets. The benchmark standardizes the prediction task and the training and testing data. It also provides a unified evaluation protocol that supports direct comparison across models. Using this framework, we provide the first comprehensive comparative evaluation of non-learning, statistical learning, and deep learning models. We show that learning-based methods clearly outperform non-learning models, with graph neural networks achieving the best mean performance, while the strongest learning-based models remain relatively close to one another. Beyond aggregate mean absolute error (MAE) and root mean squared error (RMSE), the framework also provides breakdowns by prediction horizon and delay change, enabling more detailed analysis of model behavior across forecasting regimes.

### [236] [Learning What Not to Impute: An Uncertainty-Aware Diffusion Framework for Meaningful Missingness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05073)
*Lixing Zhang,Yidong Ouyang,Weifu Li,Shixiang Zhu,Guang Cheng,Liyan Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统缺失值填充忽略“有意义缺失”的问题，本文提出了Diff-Joint框架，利用扩散模型联合建模数据与缺失掩码，实现了对数据缺失属性的精准识别与填充，显著改善了数据分析的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的缺失值填充方法通常假设所有缺失值都是由于观测失败导致的，忽略了部分数据本身就是“有意义缺失”（即本身不存在或在语义上为空）的情况。为了解决这种混淆，研究者提出了选择性填充（Selective imputation）问题，旨在同时识别哪些缺失项应当保留，哪些应当进行预测填充。

Method: 提出了一种基于扩散模型（Diffusion-based）的框架Diff-Joint。该方法通过联合建模表格数据与潜在的缺失掩码（Latent missingness mask），采用条件采样与不确定性感知聚合交替进行，实现对缺失值填充与缺失状态（即是否需要填充）的迭代优化。

Result: 在合成数据集和真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，Diff-Joint能够有效识别有意义的缺失项，在保持竞争力的填充精度的同时，显著提升了下游机器学习任务的性能。

Conclusion: 本研究通过Diff-Joint框架成功解决了数据中“有意义缺失”与“观测缺失”的区分问题，证明了联合建模缺失机制与数据内容对于提升数据质量和下游任务性能的重要性。

Abstract: Missing value imputation is a fundamental task in machine learning, with most existing methods assuming that all missing entries correspond to unobserved regular values. In many real-world datasets, however, missingness may arise from two distinct sources: some entries are meaningfully missing (intrinsically absent and semantically valid), while others are missing due to the observation process and should be imputed. We formalize this distinction as a selective imputation problem, where the goal is to jointly infer which missing entries should be preserved and which should be recovered. To address this challenge, we propose Diff-Joint, a diffusion-based framework that jointly models tabular data together with a latent missingness mask. The method alternates between conditional sampling and uncertainty-aware aggregation to iteratively refine both imputed values and missingness labels. Empirical results on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that Diff-Joint effectively identifies meaningfully missing entries while achieving competitive imputation accuracy and improved downstream task performance.

</details>


### [237] [Identifying Gems from Roman RAPIDly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05103)
*Karan Gandhi,Ashish A. Mahabal,Jacob E. Jencson,Russ R. Laher,Ben Rusholme,Lin Yan,Ryan M. Lau,Schuyler D. Van Dyk,Mansi M. Kasliwal*

Result: 实验结果表明，RuBR 模型在识别真实瞬变源方面表现出高有效性。特别是通过领域自适应（DA）策略，模型展现了在缺乏早期任务真实标签的情况下，依然能实现稳健的实时瞬变源与虚假信号分类的潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的 RuBR 模型和方法论在缺乏真实观测数据的情况下，为南希·格蕾丝·罗曼空间望远镜的实时瞬变源识别提供了可靠的解决方案。其结合领域自适应的训练策略有效应对了数据分布差异，为任务初期的数据处理奠定了基础。

Abstract: The Nancy Grace Roman Space Telescope (Roman), set for launch as early as September 2026, will conduct wide-field infrared imaging surveys with unprecedented spatial resolution and cadence, enabling the discovery of millions of astronomical transients. Hence, it is necessary to have automated pipelines for generating alerts in place so that the telescope can begin discovering reliable transients and variable objects soon after it is launched. However, no real Roman data currently exist, making the development of such pipelines difficult. In this work, we present a machine learning model $RuBR$ and a general methodology for distinguishing genuine transient and variable detections from spurious (bogus) detections within the RAPID pipeline. In particular, we present three models using this methodology: $RuBR_{comb}$ trained and tested on combined locally injected and OpenUniverse2024 transients, $RuBR_{loc}$ trained on locally injected transients and tested on OpenUniverse2024 transients, and $RuBR_{DA}$ that combines locally injected transients with a fraction of OpenUniverse2024 transients in domain-adaptation mode for training. This paves the way for strategies to adapt the $RuBR_{comb}$ model to real observations in the absence of any ground-truth labels during the early phases of the Roman mission. While the image differencing pipeline continues to be improved, our experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach and its promise for robust real-bogus classification in the Roman era.

### [238] [RePercENT: Scaling Disentangled Representation Learning Beyond Two Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05109)
*Vasiliki Rizou,Pascal Frossard,Dorina Thanou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 RePercENT 框架，打破了多模态解耦仅限于双模态的扩展性限制，通过即插即用的自监督方法高效分离共享与特有特征，并在多项任务中验证了其计算效率与性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多模态解耦方面主要局限于双模态场景，存在扩展性瓶颈；此外，为了挖掘模态间的全方位交互而不丢失特定模态的信息，需要一种能够高效、可扩展地实现多模态解耦的方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 RePercENT 的自监督框架，该框架采用即插即用架构直接作用于预提取的嵌入向量，无需大规模联合预训练。方法引入了联合优化目标，用以同时派生出模态间的共享组件和模态特有的组件，并提供了相应的理论最优性保证。

Result: 实验表明，RePercENT 在跨多种模态和任务的场景下，能够成功恢复出解耦的表示成分，在保持竞争性性能的同时，大幅降低了计算复杂度。

Conclusion: RePercENT 通过一种即插即用的架构实现了多模态表示的解耦，为处理超过两种模态的数据提供了一种高效、可扩展且具备理论保障的解决方案，能够有效地提取共享与特有特征，同时显著降低计算成本。

Abstract: To leverage the full potential of multimodal data, we need representations that go beyond the state-of-the-art alignment and fusion approaches and exploit all cross-modal interactions without sacrificing modality-specific information. Learning disentangled representations is a principled way to identify these underlying shared and unique factors that are hidden in observational data. However, while multimodal disentanglement is a compelling paradigm, existing methods are largely confined to the two-modality regime due to its inherent scalability bottleneck. To address this, we propose RePercENT, a self-supervised framework designed to surpass these limitations and unlocks scalable pairwise disentanglement beyond two modalities. Through a multimodal `plug-and-play' architecture, our approach operates directly on pre-extracted embeddings, eliminating the need for extensive joint pre-training while making no assumptions regarding the underlying modalities or foundation model backbones. Moreover, we introduce a joint optimization objective for simultaneously deriving the shared and unique components, and provide formal theoretical guarantees that characterize the optimality of our solution. Across diverse modalities and tasks, RePercENT successfully recovers disentangled components while maintaining competitive performance and significantly reducing computational complexity.
