### [239] [Graph Set Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05116)
*Jose E. Escrig Molina,Baoquan Chen,Daniel Probst*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 Graph Set Transformer (GST) 的架构，通过在网络层内交织节点级图结构与跨图集合上下文，有效克服了传统图集学习中特征提取与上下文建模分离带来的信息瓶颈，显著提升了在多种图集预测任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图集（set of graphs）学习方法（如 DeepSets 或 SetTransformer）通常依赖于预先计算的图嵌入，这种“先提取后聚合”的分离式架构会在特征提取与集合级上下文建模之间形成瓶颈，难以捕捉依赖于集合背景的局部结构特征。因此，研究者旨在开发一种能够同时处理节点局部信息与全局上下文的集成模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Graph Set Transformer (GST) 的新型架构。与传统先用 GNN 提取特征再进行集合处理的方法不同，GST 将节点级别的特征传播与跨图的上下文建模在每一层中进行交织，并利用门控机制（gating mechanism）动态融合这两类信息，从而实现了局部结构与全局背景的深度耦合。

Result: 在合成数据集及包括反应中心识别、反应产率预测和图像分类在内的三个实际任务中，GST 在参数预算相同的情况下，表现均优于现有的基线模型。消融实验证实，这种将局部和集合上下文交织的设计是其性能提升的核心因素。

Conclusion: Graph Set Transformer (GST) 通过在每一层中交织局部图结构信息与全局集合上下文，证明了这种一体化处理模式优于传统的“先特征提取、后集合建模”的级联架构，是处理复杂图集任务的有效范式。

Abstract: We introduce the Graph Set Transformer (GST), a neural network architecture for learning on sets of graphs, designed for tasks in which per-element predictions depend on set-wide context as well as local structure. Existing architectures, including DeepSets and SetTransformer, require pre-encoded graph embeddings from a separate GNN, creating a bottleneck between feature extraction and set-level contextualisation. In contrast, GST interleaves node-level feature propagation and cross-graph contextual modelling at every layer, fusing the two levels of information through a gating mechanism. We evaluate GST on a controlled synthetic suite designed to isolate set-conditional structural reasoning and on three real-data benchmarks spanning per-atom reaction-centre identification, reaction yield prediction, and image classification. Under matched parameter budgets, GST performs better than the baselines across these settings. An architectural ablation strongly suggests that the interleaving of local and set context contributes substantially to this advantage.

### [240] [Deep Embedded Multiplicative DMD for Algebra-Preserving Koopman Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05131)
*Kelan Gray,Finlay Brown,Nicolas Boullé,Matthew J. Colbrook*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DeepMDMD结合了深度学习与算子代数约束，通过在可学习的潜空间内精确强制执行Koopman乘法规则，显著提升了高维非线性动力系统建模的紧凑性、动态一致性和抗噪性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Koopman方法存在权衡：深度学习方法虽然灵活但缺乏结构约束，而结构保持方法往往依赖于预定义的固定字典。本文旨在解决如何通过学习更具表现力的非线性坐标，同时精确地强制执行Koopman算子的代数属性，以改善模型在处理复杂非线性动力学时的表现。

Method: 提出深度嵌入乘法动态模式分解（DeepMDMD）。该方法结合了深度学习的可学习坐标和结构保持方法的代数约束，通过交替训练策略：一是执行精确的乘法算子更新，二是执行可微的潜空间聚类，以强制满足Koopman乘法规则（闭包性质）。

Result: DeepMDMD在多个动力学系统（如哈密顿系统、混沌系统及流体力学）中表现优异。相比传统方法，它能学习到更紧凑的字典，减少频谱污染，揭示更丰富的连续谱结构。在高维流场（如圆柱绕流和带噪盖板驱动腔流）实验中，即便在强噪声干扰下，DeepMDMD依然能保持稳健的长期预测和相干结构。

Conclusion: DeepMDMD提供了一种有效的Koopman学习范式：即“学习坐标，约束代数”。该方法通过在学习到的潜空间中强制执行乘法代数结构，实现了比传统方法更紧凑、更具动态连贯性的字典表示，为处理高维、非线性及含噪动力系统提供了一种稳健的框架。

Abstract: Koopman theory turns nonlinear dynamics into a linear spectral problem. In computation, however, everything depends on a hard finite-dimensional choice: the observables must be expressive, nearly invariant under the dynamics, and, ideally, compatible with composition. Deep Koopman methods learn flexible coordinates, whereas structure-preserving methods enforce operator identities on fixed dictionaries. We combine these ideas by introducing Deep Embedded Multiplicative Dynamic Mode Decomposition (DeepMDMD), a method that learns a latent space and a partition of it, while enforcing the Koopman product rule as an exact algebraic constraint. Training alternates between an exact multiplicative operator update and a differentiable latent-clustering step that promotes Koopman closure. The result is a finite transition map on learned latent cells. Its nonzero spectrum lies on the unit circle, its dictionary is shaped by the dynamics rather than by ambient geometry, and forecasts are made in latent coordinates before being decoded to physical space. Across Hamiltonian, chaotic, and fluid examples, DeepMDMD learns dictionaries that are far more compact and dynamically coherent than those produced by geometric MDMD partitions. It reduces spectral pollution, reveals richer continuous-spectrum structure, and gives stable forecasts under severe noise. In high-dimensional flows, including a 158,624-dimensional cylinder wake and a noisy $Re=20,000$ lid-driven cavity, it preserves coherent structures and long-time spectral statistics where state-space MDMD fails. These results suggest a practical rule for Koopman learning: learn the coordinates, constrain the algebra.

</details>


### [241] [Generating Financial Time Series by Matching Random Convolutional Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05138)
*Konrad J. Mueller,Nikita Zozoulenko,Ben Wood,Thomas Cass,Lukas Gonon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可微的随机卷积特征映射SOCK，解决了金融时间序列生成中因样本稀缺导致的过拟合和特征捕捉能力不足问题，显著提升了生成模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融时间序列样本稀缺，现有基于对抗训练的方法容易过拟合，而基于路径签名（path signatures）的方法在捕捉序列特征时存在截断深度限制，难以有效表征复杂金融数据。

Method: 提出了一种名为SOCK（SOft Competing Kernels）的全可微随机卷积特征映射方法，通过匹配生成数据与真实数据在SOCK特征空间下的分布差异来引导生成器训练，从而避免了传统随机卷积核不可微的问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多个小样本金融数据集上，使用SOCK训练的生成器在生成质量上优于路径签名和扩散模型基线；同时，SOCK在双样本假设检验和时间序列分类任务中表现优异，具备很强的特征表达能力。

Conclusion: SOCK作为一种可微的随机卷积特征映射，能够有效解决金融时间序列生成中因小样本导致的过拟合问题，在生成质量和下游任务性能上均优于现有的路径签名及扩散模型基线。

Abstract: Generating realistic financial time series is challenging as training data is often limited to a single historical path. With such scarce data, overfitting is hard to avoid, especially under adversarial training where a trained discriminator can memorize the training samples. To mitigate this, recent approaches train generators to minimize the discrepancy between untrained feature representations of real and generated time series. In these works, the feature maps are based on path signatures, which can fail to capture relevant time series properties at tractable truncation depths. In this work, we instead train generators by matching random convolutional features of real and generated time series. Existing random convolutional feature maps, such as Rocket and Hydra, have been shown to provide informative representations of real-world time series, but cannot supervise generative models because they are non-differentiable. We introduce SOCK (SOft Competing Kernels), a fully differentiable random convolutional feature map, suited to train generative time series models. We show that generators trained by matching random SOCK features consistently outperform signature and diffusion baselines across a wide range of small-sample financial datasets. We further demonstrate SOCK's expressiveness on two-sample hypothesis testing and time series classification tasks, where SOCK matches or outperforms existing unsupervised feature maps.

</details>


### [242] [BBOmix: A Tabular Benchmark for Hyperparameter Optimization of Unsupervised Biological Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05139)
*Luca Thale-Bombien,Jan Ewald,Ralf König,Aaron Klein*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个针对生物多组学数据无监督表示学习的开源超参数优化基准BBOmix，通过大规模实验评估了多种自编码器架构和优化方法，为生物信息学中的自动模型调优提供了重要参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高通量测序产生的多组学数据维度极高，自编码器（AE）是降维的关键工具。然而，AE对超参数极度敏感，传统的无监督重构损失往往无法准确反映下游生物学任务的性能，且穷举式超参数搜索计算成本昂贵，导致研究者常使用次优配置。因此，需要一个针对无监督生物表示学习的开源基准来优化配置选择过程。

Method: 构建了包含105,000次评估的基准数据集，涵盖了4种自编码器（AE）架构和来自TCGA与SCHC数据集的7种多组学模态；量化了重构损失与下游任务性能之间的相关性；评估了多种单保真度、多保真度及迁移学习超参数优化（HPO）算法。

Result: BBOmix成功构建了大规模的无监督表示学习评估基准；研究发现重构损失并非下游任务性能的完美代理指标；通过对现有HPO方法的全面对比，验证了在生物信息学任务中利用该基准进行模型配置优化的有效性。

Conclusion: BBOmix为无监督生物表示学习的超参数优化研究提供了首个开源基准，揭示了重构损失与下游任务性能之间复杂的非线性关系，证明了开发针对特定领域任务的优化策略的必要性，并为未来该领域的方法评估树立了严谨的基准。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of high-throughput sequencing has led to large, high-dimensional omics datasets. Deep unsupervised learning architectures, particularly Autoencoders (AEs), are increasingly used for dimensionality reduction and representation learning in this domain. However, AEs are highly sensitive to architectural choices and hyperparameters, and unsupervised optimization typically relies on reconstruction loss, which may be a poor proxy for downstream utility. Exhaustive hyperparameter optimization (HPO) is computationally expensive, leading researchers to frequently rely on suboptimal default configurations. To democratize access to large-scale unsupervised HPO research, we introduce $\textbf{BBOmix}$, the first open-source tabular benchmark for unsupervised representation learning on real-world biological data. Our benchmark includes 105,000 evaluations across four AE architectures and seven multi-omics modalities from the TCGA and SCHC datasets. We quantify the correlation between reconstruction loss and downstream task performance and provide an extensive evaluation of state-of-the-art single-fidelity, multi-fidelity, and transfer learning HPO methods, establishing a rigorous baseline for future research in unsupervised biological representation learning.

</details>
